Harbin Strange Robbery Case 83

▲ Bandits Rob the Residence of the Director of the Eastern Railway

▲ Police Squad of Three Hundred Surrounds for Six Hours

▲ Holding the Victim's Family Hostage, They Leave by Car

Harbin Correspondence: Since the Northeast fell into the hands of the Japanese army, military connections have been established. As of August, the people have lost their land, workers have lost their jobs, and scholars have lost their schools. The decline of society is becoming increasingly extreme. Major ports such as Jilin, Changchun, Liaoning, and Harbin are all experiencing commercial depression and market downturn. Therefore, the number of unemployed people is increasing daily. Those with lofty aspirations and a desire for revenge go to join the volunteer army and carry out the movement to restore the country. Those of lesser ambition, in order to solve their current living problems, engage in banditry. As a result, bandits are rampant everywhere. Even in Harbin, despite the Japanese army's rampaging and dense network of henchmen, several robbery cases occur every day. The puppet state's police exhaust their efforts but cannot prevent them. On the 11th of this month, the residence of Zhang Shu, the puppet director of the Eastern Railway, was also visited by four bandits. Although they did not steal any property, the bandits confronted the surrounding police, numbering over three hundred, for six hours. In the end, they took the victim's family as hostages and calmly escaped. This is the largest bandit case in the Northeast in recent times and must be recorded. Zhang Shu was the chief of staff when Sun Liechen was the military governor of Jilin and is one of the old Northeastern soldiers. He has served as a director of the Eastern Railway for several years, even serving as director last year. After the September 18th Incident in Shenyang, Zhang had a close relationship with Xi Qia and strongly supported Xi Qia's plan to become the puppet Jilin governor. When Ding and Li resisted Japan in Harbin, Zhang secretly helped Xi Qia to overthrow Ding and Li. After the establishment of the puppet state, he had almost become one of the founding heroes. It is a pity that he has not yet obtained an important position. Wang Zhiyou, the commander-in-chief of the vanguard of the Self-Defense Army, was lured to Harbin by Zhang because of their close relationship, and was placed under house arrest and not allowed to return. This caused the Ding-Xing Self-Defense Army to lose a senior commander responsible for directing the army, and it was eventually defeated by the Japanese army. Therefore, from Zhang's personal perspective, he is a loyal minister of the puppet state and a good friend of Xi Qia. But from the perspective of us, the divine Chinese descendants, he is, without a doubt, the number one Chinese traitor. Zhang obtained the position of puppet director of the Eastern Railway because of this, with a very generous monthly salary. His residence is located at No. 47 Gongsiju Street in Nangang, Eastern Railway, in a ten-story Western-style building, living in extreme luxury. On the morning of the 11th, at 7:00 AM, Zhang had not yet gotten out of bed when two middle-aged men, both wearing blue serge Western suits and hats, one resembling the owner and the other resembling a follower, arrived at Zhang's door. They went up the steps and rang the doorbell. The doorman came out to answer. The one resembling the owner held

Page 11

Page 12

Important News 84

a letter, writing "[Director Zhang's regards]" and gave it to Zhang, claiming to have been sent by Zhang Zuoxiang and had confidential matters to see Director Zhang. The doorman replied that the owner was not up yet, and the guest was invited inside to wait. The doorman did not dare to refuse and invited them into the living room. At this time, two other men, both around 24 or 25 years old, one wearing a blue serge Western suit and the other wearing a blue cloth gown, resembling students, walked in through the back door of Zhang's residence. Zhang's servant caught a glimpse of them and immediately greeted them with a knife, asking what they were doing. The two men claimed to be secret agents from the Japanese Military Police Department, saying that they had just seen two suspicious-looking people enter the residence, that these two people were from Fengtian and were reactionaries, and that they needed to be arrested. The servant did not understand the truth and allowed them to enter the house. The two men also greeted the two street police officers guarding the back door to come in, as if asking for their assistance. At this time, the first two men were still in the living room. The letter they claimed was from Zhang Zuoxiang was taken by a maid and sent to Zhang Shu's bedroom. Zhang opened the letter and discovered many suspicious points. Just as he was wondering and about to put on his clothes to ask, the two men who had arrived later were also invited into the living room by the servant. After the two groups of guests met, they suddenly drew their guns, ordering the servants not to move and disarming the two street police officers. Because of the noise, a maid in the outer room heard it and rushed into Zhang Shu's bedroom to report. Upon hearing the news, Zhang immediately locked the bedroom door and jumped out of the back window, running to the nearby Industrial University to borrow a telephone and report to various parties. Soon, the entire puppet police brigade, the garrison team, the detective team, and the Third Office, totaling about three hundred people, rushed to the scene and surrounded Zhang's residence several times, intending to open fire and attack. At this time, the bandits searched for Zhang Shu inside and could not find him. Seeing the police surrounding the area, they knew that the matter had been exposed. They immediately forced Zhang's family members into the living room, forbidding them from moving, and sent a servant to shout outside the door, saying that if the police opened fire, they would completely kill Zhang's family members. At this time, Zhang Shu was also in the street, hearing this, he was extremely frightened and hurriedly persuaded the police not to open fire. The police complied with the victim's request, only taking a surrounding posture and remotely monitoring. This stalemate lasted for a long time. The bandits could not escape, and the police did not dare to open fire. The Japanese military police heard the news at 11:30 AM and arrived with more than twenty people, also intending to open fire. However, after Zhang Shu's pleading and request for them to retreat, the Japanese military police immediately withdrew. Around 12:00 PM, the bandits searched from one room and found Zhang's friend Wang Zhiyou (former commander-in-chief of the Jilin Self-Defense Army, currently the deputy minister of the Xi Qia army's Harbin Special Service Department) and demanded that Wang go outside to tell Zhang to prepare 10,000 yuan in cash, 20,000 rounds of ammunition, and that the police immediately retreat and send a special car for them to leave, otherwise there would be trouble. Wang went outside to tell Zhang, but Zhang had no way to arrange it and immediately sent Cheng Delin, the patrol chief of the Third Office, inside to persuade the bandits that cash and ammunition were not easy to arrange, but that the police could retreat and a special car could be sent. The bandits initially refused, but because the stalemate had lasted too long, many Chinese and foreigners were gathered on the street to watch, fearing other changes, they only asked Zhang to prepare a small car to send them away. The police team immediately retreated, and Zhang complied. Subsequently, the detectives, according to Zhang's request, completely withdrew. Zhang also offered a price of 1,500 yuan to hire a small car to transport them, but no one dared to respond. Later, Wang Zhiyou summoned the military special service department's car number two and drove it into Zhang's courtyard. The bandits ordered the driver to lower the window curtains and park in the center of the courtyard. First, they had a servant get into the car. After ten minutes, seeing no movement, they ordered him out of the car. Then, they ordered another servant to get into the car. After another ten minutes, they had him get out. The two bandits then got into the car. Shortly after, the other two bandits took Zhang's relatives, Liu and Wang, into the car, and with their guns, forced the driver to drive away at full speed. By this time, it was 1:25 PM. When the car passed the street corner, the Chinese and Russian onlookers were in a sea of people, shouting and applauding. Later, the car drove to Xiangfang, where the bandits got out of the car. More than ten people were waiting for them, and they took the four bandits away. Before leaving, the bandits handed over a pistol seized from the street police officer to the driver and told him to take it back. When the bandits got into the car, two bandits changed into the blue gowns of the servants, and took out 200 yuan in cash from a pocket and placed it on the table. They left calmly, without taking anything. Therefore, some people say that the four were not bandits, but members of the Self-Defense Army or Volunteer Army. (11th)

Xu Yuanquan and Others 85

Return to Hankou After the Lushan Conference

▲ Xiao Zhichu Briefly Talks About the Conference Situation

▲ Chiang to Increase Two Divisions to Assist in Suppressing Hubei Bandits

▲ Guangji County Magistrate Relieved of Post for Losing City and Sent to the Province for Trial

Hankou Correspondence: The Lushan Conference, which began on the 14th, lasted for three consecutive days. The general direction for diplomacy, finance, and military affairs has been largely decided. Xu Yuanquan, the director of Qingxiang in Hubei Province, along with Xiao Zhichu, commander of the 44th Division, Yu Feipeng, vice minister of the Ministry of Transportation, Qian Zongze, vice minister of the Ministry of Railways, He Jingwu, director of the Pinghan Railway Bureau, Lin Xiang, director of the Transportation Department of the General Headquarters, and others, left the mountain and returned to Hankou on the Jiangjing Steamer. They arrived at the port at 1:00 PM on the 17th. Xu felt slightly ill due to fatigue along the way and returned to his private residence to rest after arriving. According to Xiao Zhichu, he briefly said: "This time I went to Xunyang to meet Chairman Chiang and report on the bandit suppression situation in Hubei Province. Chairman Chiang said that the armies of Hubei Province have worked hard to suppress the bandits and have suffered many casualties. Many brigade and regimental commanders have also been injured. In addition to praising them, he was very concerned and ordered them to maintain their determination and continue to work hard to completely eliminate the remaining bandits. As for the Lushan gathering, in addition to military and political personnel from Hubei Province, Chairman He Yunqiao (Jian) from Hunan Province, Minister He Jingzhi (Yingqin) from Jiangxi Province, Chairman Xiong Tianyi (Shihui), Army Commander Chen Xiucheng, and others from the capital, such as Dean Wang and others, also went by plane. There was a detailed discussion on military, financial, diplomatic, and bandit suppression matters. In military affairs, uniformity was sought, and the regulations of the Military Commission were used as a unit, with each army directly commanding two divisions. If a certain division had a large number of people, another division would be formed, and military expenses would also be increased appropriately. In order to thoroughly eliminate the bandits in Hubei, Chairman Chiang will also increase the 10th Division of Wei Lihuang and the 83rd Division of Jiang Fusheng to Hubei to assist in the suppression. Wan Yaohuang's 13th Division will advance towards Jingshan to assist the 10th Army in searching and suppressing the remaining bandits in central Hubei. The defense of the southern section of the Pinghan Railway will be filled by the 89th Division of Tang Enbo. Director He Xuezhuan will meet with Director Liu Xueya and then go down the mountain and return to Hankou. Civil Affairs Director Zhu Huaibing and Construction Director Li Shucheng will return together after the joint meeting. I will stay in Hankou for three days and then go to Yingcheng to command." It is reported that the weather in Lushan has recently turned cold, and everyone is sick. Chiang is also slightly ill and will come to Hankou only after all plans have been completely decided. Xia Douyin will be able to return to Hankou on the 19th. Wan Yaohuang took the Jiangshun steamer west on the 17th and will arrive on the 18th. Finance Director Shen Zhaonian went to Nanjing on the 17th on Xia Douyin's orders to pay respects to Finance Minister Song Ziwen and request an increase in subsidies. If Song had not returned to Beijing, he would also go to Shanghai.

The military situation for bandit suppression in Hubei Province has remained tense in recent days. In eastern Hubei, Xu Xiangqian's puppet Fourth Front Army of the Red Army has withdrawn from the county seat of Guangji due to pressure from the army and air force. The 47th Division has now all arrived in Wuxue, and part of it has been stationed in Guangji, coordinating with local gentry to handle the aftermath. County Magistrate Dong of the county has been relieved of his post for losing the county seat. Chairman Chiang ordered the Pacification Headquarters to instruct Shangguan Yunxiang to transfer the troops stationed in Guangji and send him to the province for trial. The vacancy will be filled by a capable person. In western and central Hubei, the battle between the army and the bandits is even more fierce. He Long personally led Wang Yuming's puppet 7th Division to occupy the area around Su Lake in Qianjiang. Duan Yulin's puppet 8th Division occupied Jingshan, and Duan Dechang's puppet 9th Division occupied Zhangjiegang. He Long and Wang Lingji's Sichuan army are in a stalemate, and Duan and Zhang Zhenhan's division are in a stalemate. According to reports from the front, Wang's troops have won successive victories after recovering Qianjiang and are now fiercely attacking Su Lake. Wang himself has moved from Yichang to Shashi to supervise the suppression and has telegraphed Liu Xiang to increase the dispatch of two brigades to Hubei to assist in the suppression. Zhang's division recovered Yuxin River. On the 14th, they fought a bloody battle with the bandits at Sanwen River and Huanxin River. The bandits were unable to withstand the attack and retreated towards Tanbutou and Zhangjiegang. On the 15th, the division issued a general attack order, supervised by Division Commander Zhang Zhenhan. After a long and fierce battle, the 25th Regiment of the puppet 9th Division reinforced the front line, and the 22nd, 23rd, and 24th Regiments of the puppet 8th Division also arrived at the river bank to confront the government troops. On the 16th, Zhang Zhenhan still supervised the Meng and Niu Regiments to charge with bayonets, engaging in repeated hand-to-hand combat, and broke through the Red Army's Caijia Temple position. The bandits then retreated in droves, and the government troops successively occupied Huangjiatai, Qingle Temple, and Chenjiazu areas. At that time, it was raining heavily, and it was difficult to move the troops, so they were unable to pursue. As soon as the weather clears, they will continue to search and suppress. (June 17)

Southern Jiangxi 86

Bandit Suppression and Pacification

▲ Guangdong Army Moves Troops to Monitor Bandit Gangs in Eastern Jiangxi

▲ Xie Yuanhan Appointed Pacification Commissioner of Southern Jiangxi

Guangzhou Correspondence: The communist bandits in Zhangzhou, after withdrawing, intended to return to their base camp in eastern Jiangxi, and the areas of Xinfeng, Longnan, and Qiannan in southern Jiangxi are actually close to the bandit areas in eastern Jiangxi. The original garrison in Xinfeng was the 4th Division of the 2nd Guangdong Army, led by Zhang Meixin. Zhang recently came to the province to discuss official matters with Chen Jitang. It was recently heard that the bandits in eastern Jiangxi were rampant, so he took the Yuehan train to Shao on the morning of the 10th, carrying a large number of military supplies. He transported them to Jiangxi by land from Shao. Zhang himself first returned to Xinfeng by plane from Shao. It is heard that the task of Zhang's division will focus on the San Nan area, and a certain unit will be transferred from the First Army to Xinfeng to assist in the defense. In addition, the suppression of Peng Dehuai and Li Mingrui's two bandit gangs in western Jiangxi will be carried out by the Second Division and the Independent First Brigade to cut off the connection between Peng and Li's bandits and the various gangs in eastern Jiangxi. It was found that after Peng and Li's two gangs were defeated and fled to Guidong County in eastern Hunan, the 2nd Division of the 1st Guangdong Army, led by Ye Zhao, advanced to Chongyi, and the 2nd Division's training regiment stationed at Changmeisi, led by Deng Qichang, also joined the 4th Battalion of the division and crossed the Jiangkou to pursue them. They cleared the remaining bandits in the area. According to a telegram report from the regiment, the regiment and Xiao Battalion of the 4th Regiment were ordered to go to the Guobu area to suppress the communist bandits. Upon arriving at the destination, they searched everywhere. More than a thousand bandits were defeated. On the 7th, the Hunan army and our army surrounded the bandits in two directions. The battle was fierce. It is estimated that countless bandits were killed in the battle, and many weapons were seized. The remaining bandits were defeated and scattered. Currently, there is no food in Guotian Guobu and other places in Chongyi. All food is transported from Nanxiong and Dayu. It was also heard that Yu Hanmou recently convened a military meeting in Nan'an to discuss and decide on the second phase of the communist suppression plan. As for the seventeen counties in southern Jiangxi, since the Guangdong army recovered them, the local area has not yet recovered from the devastation, and everything is waiting to be rebuilt. Yu Hanmou has also ordered his subordinates to rush to handle the aftermath and pacification matters. At the same time, he plans to build a highway from Ganzhou through Nan'an to Dayu on the Guangdong border, to accommodate the refugees in the area and provide work as relief. As for the aftermath and pacification, the Southern Jiangxi Seventeen Counties Pacification Office has been established as the presiding authority. The central government has appointed Xie Yuanhan, the former governor of Jiangxi Province, as the pacification commissioner. Xie traveled south from Shanghai a month ago, passing through Guangzhou, and then went to Nanxiong, and then took a sedan chair from Yuling to take office in southern Jiangxi. (June 13)

Jiangsu Provincial Government 87

Drafts Financial Management Plan

▲ Gu Zhutong Goes to Beijing to Meet with the Central Government

▲ If the Result is Satisfactory, the Intention to Resign Can be Dismissed

Governor Gu Zhutong and all the members of the Jiangsu Provincial Government resigned en masse due to financial difficulties. After the State Council resolved to send a telegram to express their condolences and retain them, they were instructed to propose a plan to reorganize the finances. It is now learned that the provincial government, after receiving the order, has already drafted the plan, and its contents are divided into six items: (1) Salt tax (2) Surtax on tobacco and alcohol (designated for road construction) (3) Special business tax (4) Recovery of liquor license tax for self-management (5) Transformation of ordinary business tax into business license tax (6) Clearing of land tax, starting with clearing the land area, and selecting five counties for pilot implementation, to be completed within six months. This plan was taken to Nanjing by Gu Zhutong and Zhou FoHai yesterday afternoon to discuss with President Wang. Whether or not Governor Gu and others can dismiss their resignation will depend on whether the plan can be adopted and implemented by the central government. According to Finance Director Shu Shifu's statement to reporters, the financial reorganization plan proposed by the provincial government this time does have some violations of the central government's regulations and increases the burden on the people, but Jiangsu Province's finances have reached the end of their rope, and there is really no other way.

Shanghai-Songhu War Zone 88

Outline of the Organization of the Post-War Reconstruction Preparatory Committee

The State Council promulgated the outline of the organization of the Shanghai-Songhu War Zone Post-War Reconstruction Preparatory Committee on the 18th. The original text is as follows: (1) The National Government will establish the Shanghai-Songhu War Zone Post-War Reconstruction Preparatory Committee to prepare for the post-war reconstruction and revitalization of the Shanghai-Songhu War Zone. (2) The committee will be organized by 27 members appointed by the National Government. One person will be designated as the chairman, and three people will be mutually elected as standing committee members. (3) The committee members' meetings will be convened by the chairman. (4) The committee will set up four groups: design, review, finance, and epidemic prevention, with each committee member serving in a group. The rules of procedure will be determined separately. (5) After the committee's proposal is resolved, it will be submitted to the government for approval and implementation. (6) The committee may entrust local post-war reconstruction agencies to investigate matters that the committee should investigate. (7) The committee will have one secretary-general and several secretarial staff. The specific rules will be determined separately. (8) The committee may hire specialized committee members when necessary. (9) If there are any matters that should be added or amended in this outline, the committee will revise it and submit it to the government for approval. (10) This outline will be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation by the National Government.

Hunan Province Plans to Build New Prisons Throughout the Province 89

▲ Nine New Prisons to be Completed in Five Years

▲ Total Cost of One Million Yuan

Changsha Correspondence: Chen Changzu, the former president of the Hunan Higher Court, vigorously planned to build a new prison in the provincial capital during his tenure to improve the judiciary. He sold the land of the old Changsha prison and the Zixin Institute and obtained more than 100,000 yuan. He also obtained 100,000 yuan from the Ministry of Justice and planned to build the first new prison outside the North Gate. Construction was underway when he suddenly received an order from the ministry to be transferred to the president of the Hubei Higher Court, and Xu Shengjin succeeded him as president of the Hunan Court. Xu took office in Hunan last month. Because building a new prison is an important measure for regaining jurisdiction over foreign affairs, he still plans to actively complete the first new prison in Changsha. He will also divide the entire province into nine districts and build a total of nine new prisons. It is expected to be completed within five years at a total cost of approximately one million yuan. All judicial expenses allocated by the Ministry will be withheld and used. If it is not enough, the Hunan Provincial Government will provide subsidies. Yang XuanYou has been appointed to be responsible for planning the construction of new prisons throughout the province. The construction sites and the number of prisoners to be accommodated are recorded as follows: (1) The first new prison will be located in Changsha, with a capacity of 1,000 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Liuyang, Liling, Ningxiang, Xiangyin, Xiangtan, Yiyang, Youxian, Chaling, and Anhua. (2) The second new prison will be located in Chenxian, with a capacity of 500 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Guiyang, Linwu, Xuanzhang, Rucheng, Guidong, Zixing, Jiahe, Lanshan, and Yongxing. (3) The third new prison will be located in Yuanling, with a capacity of 300 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Chenxi, Yupu, Luxi, Baojing, Yongshun, Longshan, Sangzhi, Qiancheng, Guzhang, and Yongsui. (4) The fourth new prison will be located in Hengyang, with a capacity of 500 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Hengshan, Anren, Leiyang, Changning, and Youxian. (5) The fifth new prison will be located in Changde, with a capacity of 500 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Lixian, Linli, Yuanjiang, Hanshou, Taoyuan, Shimen, Cili, and Dayong. (6) The sixth new prison will be located in Shaoyang, with a capacity of 300 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Xinning, Xinhua, Wugang, Chengbu, and Xiangxiang. (7) The seventh new prison will be located in Lingling, with a capacity of 300 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Qiyang, Daoxian, Ningyuan, Yongming, Dong'an, Jianghua, and Xintian. (8) The eighth new prison will be located in Yueyang, with a capacity of 300 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Pingjiang, Linxiang, and Huarong. (9) The ninth new prison will be located in Zhijiang, with a capacity of 300 prisoners, and will hold convicted prisoners from Fenghuang, Huitong, Jingxian, Qianyang, Mayang, Suining, Huangxian, and Tongdao. (June 16)

Work of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department 90

▲ Establishing a Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Telephone Line There was an original long-distance telephone line established by the Ministry of Transportation between Zhenjiang and Yangzhou. However, because the established line was a single iron wire, the sound quality was extremely unclear, which caused great inconvenience to the public. The Jiangsu Construction Department is now preparing to establish a Zhenjiang-Yangzhou telephone line in order to promote balanced development in both the north and south of the Yangtze River. The Zhenjiang-Yangzhou telephone line is also a trunk line connecting the north and south of the Yangtze River and should be completed as soon as possible in order to gradually expand it. It is heard that the department has drafted a plan and submitted it to the provincial government for approval in order to start the project.

▲ Planning to Establish Martyrs' Parks Xiong Martyr Chengji and other parks have not yet been completed. The provincial government meeting has decided to hand them over to the Civil Affairs and Construction Departments, ordering them to send personnel to conduct inspections, prepare plans, submit them for discussion, and prepare separately to express respect for the martyrs. The Civil Affairs and Construction Departments have already commissioned Zhu Xi, a technician from the Construction Department, to conduct inspections and handle the matter.

▲ Protecting the Honghu Great Embankment The Hongze Lake Great Embankment is a hundred miles long from north to south and more than two rods (丈) high. It is all stonework and is the first important barrier for Huaiyang. It is extremely important. It has been heard that the Yangzhou office of the Canal Workers Relief Association has received a telegram from the chief supervisor, Chen Bomeng, stating that the stonework of the Honghu Embankment is mostly incomplete, and the stone slabs on the embankment surface, broken stones, bricks, and other materials have suffered even greater losses than sixteen years ago. If it is not repaired for a long time, the entire embankment will be destroyed, etc. It immediately sent a letter to the Huaihe River Conservancy Commission transferring it to the Anhui Provincial Government for investigation and handling, and also sent a letter to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, ordering the Huaiyin County Government to protect it properly. The provincial government handed it over to the Construction Department for handling. It is heard that the department believes that the embankment is of utmost importance and cannot be neglected in the slightest. It has ordered the county government to protect it properly in order to strengthen the embankment defense.

Wuxi 93

▲厅委調查搶米風潮: Investigation of Rice-Seizing Incidents by Commissioners from the Department: Luo Chengqiao, Gao Zhen, and Hua Yinchun, commissioners from the Department of Industry, came to Wuxi from the province the day before yesterday due to the rice-seizing incidents in the county, which threatened to affect the entire county, to conduct an on-site investigation. They went directly to the county government and invited County Magistrate Chen to investigate the truth in the countryside. Because County Magistrate Chen had other important official duties, he was unable to go. The commissioners then hired a motorboat at 9:00 AM on the (17th) and sailed to Zhangjing Bridge in the 7th District and Anzhen in the 8th District to investigate. After arriving in the countryside, they met with Shen Nianhong, assistant public security officer of Zhangjing Bridge, Hua Yanfen, the head of the town, Xu Haojiu, the head of Danjia Township, Feng Aifu, the director of the Farmers' Education Center, etc. In Anzhen, they met with Zhang Zongqi, assistant to the district public office, Huang Junyu, the head of the town, and local farmers, etc., and inquired in detail about the truth of the rice-seizing incidents and the reasons for the decline of the rural economy. The general consensus was that the rural areas were densely populated, but the arable land was limited, with each household averaging only about five mu of cultivated land, and rented land accounted for more than half of that, so food was already scarce. This year's silkworm crop was poor, and the price of silk plummeted. In the Anzhen area alone, the annual income from silkworm cocoons was around 200,000 yuan, but this year it was only one-tenth or one-twelfth of that. In addition, the wheat crop was poor and the selling price was low, resulting in even greater losses. Pawnshops in the four townships, due to the tight money supply in the market, were depressing the value of goods worth one yuan to one or two jiao. Farmers, seeing this situation, have become desperate, and as a result, rice-seizing incidents have arisen. Commissioner Luo, et al., informed them that the immediate solution was relief, but the decline of the rural economy could not be restored with one or two instances of relief. The only way forward was to revive the silk industry, promote side businesses, and increase production. The County Agricultural Improvement Center is currently adding sixteen autumn silkworm rearing guidance centers, which can be contacted for implementation. After the investigation, they returned to the city. It is reported that Commissioners Luo and Gao returned to the province yesterday (18th), and Commissioner Hua Yinchun will remain in Wuxi to handle all unfinished investigations and future liaison matters.

▲ Nineteenth Route Army Disbands Iron-Blooded Army: Since the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, the Nineteenth Route Army resisted the Japanese in Shanghai, and enthusiastic people from all over organized volunteer armies and iron-blooded groups to go to Shanghai to join the Nineteenth Route Army. Commander Cai, recognizing their patriotic enthusiasm but noting that they had not received military training, assigned them to Weng Zhaoyuan, the brigade commander of the 156th Brigade, for thorough training. In the blink of an eye, four months have passed. Now that the Shanghai Incident has come to an end, and the Nineteenth Route Army has been ordered to go to Fujian to suppress bandits, the brigade is about to depart, and the former volunteer army is no longer needed. Moreover, the training period has expired, so a graduation ceremony was held a few days ago, and the student volunteer army was sent home first. All the iron-blooded troops accompanying the army were also disbanded. This army had more than 3,000 men, all composed of people from all over. In addition to the original firearms, each was equipped with a broadsword. Except for more than 1,000 people who volunteered to go to Fujian Province to suppress bandits, the rest were all sent home yesterday, each given two yuan for travel expenses. All the broadswords were allowed to be taken home. Before leaving, Brigade Commander Weng gave a sincere speech, which deeply moved the listeners.

▲ Robbery Occurs Outside the East Gate: Cai Shigen, a farmer from Youdu Li Shang Ma Dun outside the East Gate, was visited by a boat with four bandits armed with pistols the night before last. They opened the door under the pretext of asking for information and ransacked the place, stealing more than 100 yuan. They then went to the house of Long Ajun next door. Long, realizing what was happening, went outside to sound the gong and call for help. The bandits fled in a hurry, firing their guns to intimidate the crowd. Afterwards, the local public security sub-station was alerted and went to investigate, but the bandits had already gone far away.

Changshu 94

▲ Kidnapping Case Occurs Again in Shazhou City: At 2:00 AM on the 16th, a sand boat suddenly appeared on the river surface in Xiaosha, Changyinsha, in the Nansha District of this county. The local defense corps went to inspect it and saw many people wearing uniforms, who claimed to be patrolmen of the anti-smuggling team. The defense corps did not suspect anything. Unexpectedly, more than 20 people came ashore and rushed to the defense corps headquarters, tied up six corps members, and robbed them of four rifles and one Mauser pistol. ▲ Local Maintenance Association Concludes: Previously, due to the large number of troops gathered in the county, local agencies in this county jointly formed a local public security maintenance association to facilitate supply and reception, which lasted for three months. Now that the troops stationed in Changshu have departed one after another, the maintenance association is no longer necessary. On the afternoon of the 16th, the association convened a meeting of all its members, about 40 people, to hold a closing meeting. As for the maintenance association itself, it was decided to end on the 16th, and the accounts would be sorted out and submitted for verification. It is estimated that the cost of entertaining the troops and building fortifications, etc., totaled more than 130,000 yuan.

Yangzhou 96

▲ Proposed Measures for Opening the Guihai Embankment: The Huaiyang Flood Relief Association held an executive committee meeting at 3:00 PM on the 16th at the Yangzhou office of the Transportation and Construction Relief Committee. Executive committee members from 20 counties including Jiangdu, Gaoyou, Baoying, and Taixing, such as Hu Xianbo, and local figures such as Wang Shaohe, totaling 68 people, attended. The chairman, Han Zishi, reported the purpose of the meeting. Then, Chen Bomeng, Wu Xingyi, and 18 others successively stated in detail the advantages and disadvantages of the timing and size of the opening of the three Guihai embankments in their respective counties. In the end, they argued with each other and no result was reached. At 3:00 PM on the 17th, they resumed the discussion at the same place. Chairman Han Zishi and people from upstream and downstream argued fiercely. As a result, three points were proposed regarding the opening size and date of the Guihai three embankments: (1) Build a dike below the Sanhe Zhi embankment. (2) Within two weeks, representatives from each county should submit written opinions stating the disputed size and opening date for a decision to be made. (3) Notify the people of Siyang and Bao Ying Bao Zhizhi, who were unable to attend, to submit their opinions on schedule and participate in the discussion. The meeting then adjourned.

Shaoxing 100

▲ Zhang Chuan Hu Family Will Revise Genealogy: Zhanglou Town in Shanyin was originally a large family surnamed Hu. Since the 13th generation, the three branches of Dengke Gong Huai Chen, Huai Ying, and Huai Yu moved to Kuaiji Beipotang, Zhuji, and Wuxian County, Jiangsu. In the Huaiyu branch, the 16th generation Derun Gong of the Wenbiao Gong lineage, moved to Chongren Town in Shanxi. By the 18th generation, the Ji Lin Gong Zhao generation, it was quite prosperous. During the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty, Ji Lin Gong independently revised the family tree in Chongren. Now the Chongren branch has passed to the 21st generation. The Zong Jing Zong Ming lineage of the 19th generation is particularly developed and is preparing to continue revising the genealogy. They have sent letters to the Zhang Huai family and the various branches in Jiyang Wuxian Beipotang to participate in the revision. It is heard that the matter is being presided over by Zong Jing and Zong Ming, and a Hu family genealogy liaison office has been established at 7 Zhongfu Li, Avenue Edward VII in Shanghai.

Xiaoshan 101

▲ Salt Farmers Petition for Exemption from Miscellaneous Donations and Taxes: The seventh district of Xiaoshan is located in the sandy land along the river. In addition to planting melons, fruits, and cotton, most of the residents make a living by burning salt. In the early summer of this year, there was a major flood, and most of the plants planted in the fields were flooded away, and the saltworks were shut down, so the livelihood of the salt farmers was extremely difficult. This time, the district office is forcibly collecting self-government household donations and defense corps donations, which the people are really unable to bear. On the 15th, they jointly submitted a petition to the county government to stop the collection.

Department of Education Meeting Resolves to 103

Add Four-Year Simple Normal School

▲ Rural Normal School Changed to Six Years of Graduation

The Department of Education held a working meeting on the afternoon of the 17th and resolved to revise the Organic Law of Normal Schools, which was recorded in yesterday's telegram. It is now heard that there are many changes regarding the normal school system. The following is a summary: (1) Normal schools will recruit junior high school graduates for a three-year course of study. (2) Those specifically designed to train rural elementary school teachers will be called rural normal schools, which will recruit junior high school graduates for a three-year course of study. (3) Normal schools may have attached rural normal school departments and kindergarten normal school departments. Kindergarten normal school departments will recruit junior high school graduates for a two- or three-year course of study. (4) Normal schools and senior high schools may have attached normal school classes, which will recruit senior high school graduates for a one-year normal school training. After graduation, they may serve as elementary school teachers. (5) Normal schools and junior high schools may have attached simple normal school classes, which will recruit junior high school graduates for a one-year normal school training. After graduation, they may serve as elementary school assistant teachers or simple elementary school teachers. (6) Simple normal schools will recruit elementary school graduates for a four-year course of study. After graduation, they may serve as elementary school assistant teachers or simple elementary school teachers.

Labor University Students Issue a Declaration of Protecting the School 107

▲ Hosted the Press Yesterday

The Labor University Student School Protection Association hosted the press at 3:00 PM yesterday at the school's office. More than 20 reporters from various newspapers and news agencies attended. First, Chairman Gao Zongyi reported, stating that the Ministry of Education had recently ordered the Labor University to close down on the grounds that its past achievements were not significant and that it was difficult to recover from the losses suffered in the Shanghai war. In the short history of five years, of course, there were no significant achievements to speak of. This time, the Ministry of Education did not plan to gradually recover from the losses suffered in the war but instead ordered the school to close down, which was no different from kicking someone when they were down. All the students in the school, for the sake of the future of labor education and for the sake of the opportunity for future poor youth to study, vowed to fight with all their strength. They hoped that public opinion would uphold justice. The following is a record of the declaration of protecting the school issued by all the students:

The basic mission of the Labor University is to cultivate young people in the labor movement, train technical personnel for labor, implement the Premier's industrial plan, and establish a new foundation for labor education with the balanced development of mental and physical labor, complete the Premier's policy of agriculture and industry, and realize the main attempt of the Three People's Principles, which has long been known to society. Therefore, only by abandoning the Three People's Principles can the Labor University be closed down. On the contrary, it is the inescapable responsibility of those who are faithful to the Premier's legacy to continue to develop the Labor University regardless of any sacrifice. However, unexpectedly, our government authorities have brazenly ordered the Labor University to close down. If the reasons they hold are not intentional excuses, then they fundamentally misunderstand the meaning of the Labor University. One is that "the farm is a newly established and simply equipped, and although there are many factories, they are only suitable for training ordinary professional personnel and not suitable as a laboratory for university students." The fundamental principle of labor education lies in the balanced development of mental and physical labor. The establishment of farms and factories is to provide students with the opportunity for physical labor and to train them in corresponding labor skills. It is not like ordinary universities that specialize in academic theory and experiment. Therefore, the farms and factories that can train ordinary professional personnel are suitable, but the criticism that they are newly established and simply equipped proves that the government's responsibility is not comprehensive and cannot be used as a reason for closing down the school. The second is that "there are already national central, Zhejiang, Tongji, and Jiaotong universities in the Beijing-Hangzhou-Shanghai area, or they have established engineering colleges, or they have combined engineering and agricultural colleges." Then why should the government allow it to be established independently? The reason for its independent establishment is the same as that of the Central Military Academy and the Political School, which are training bases for personnel serving the country, so it is different from other universities in that students pay their own fees and are free of charge, and they also provide relief to poor youth in the country so that they have equal opportunities to study. Once closed down, it will not only be contrary to the government's original intention of establishing the Labor University, causing labor education in our country to be interrupted, but also lose the original intention of our students to devote themselves to the Labor University, and make it impossible for more poor youth in the future to have the opportunity to study. In addition, the impact of the war has ravaged education and increased the number of out-of-school youth. The government should be considering how to reorganize war-torn education and provide relief to out-of-school youth. Unfortunately, it has used the losses caused by the impact of the war as its main reason for suddenly closing down the Labor University, which is no different from kicking someone when they are down. Moreover, the Labor University is not the only national university that has suffered losses due to the war. Why is it so thick to some and thin to others? The intention is really not known. In short, for the sake of maintaining labor education, for the sake of relieving out-of-school youth, for the sake of realizing the Premier's industrial plan and the policy of agriculture and industry, our entire student body cannot but rise up and carry out a concerted school protection movement at this critical juncture. In addition to submitting a request to the authorities to withdraw the order to close down the school, we also hope that our compatriots throughout the country will actively assist us. This is our declaration.

Records of Knocking on the Temple Bell (2) (7) Zhai Fu Does Not Remove the Garden Grass 109

Thirty

We previously agreed to take turns providing meals. The first turn fell to Brother Chunsheng. He is working hard today, and as soon as he arrives in the countryside, he is busy preparing meals. I am fortunate enough to have a good appetite, and Brother Chunsheng insisted on pulling me along as a guest.

Before we set off, Mr. Zhu called the little brother aside and told him, "You usually eat meat but not skin. Today, you are a guest at a farmer's house, so you must abide by the rules and eat the skin together. It is not easy for farmers to use the money they earn from their blood and sweat to invite us to dinner. If you dislike the lean meat and pick the fat, and waste the edible things for nothing, then you will be disappointing their kindness." The little brother nodded.

When we arrived at Brother Chunsheng's house, we saw Old Lady Song, Secretary Li, Brother Zhao Xiaoer, and Old Man Ding were all there, and the host just filled an Eight Immortals table. Sister-in-law Chunsheng was in the kitchen preparing the food and cooking the dishes herself. Their two lovely children, Meixiang and Ying'er, were busy making tea, serving dishes, adding rice, and handing out hand towels. The dishes served tonight were four bowls and four plates. The plates were dried shreds, pickles, duck eggs, and sausages; the bowls were vegetable tofu soup, pickled carp, stewed chicken, and braised pork. We only get to eat this kind of dish once every few months in our countryside. Tonight's dishes were especially hearty and rich, served in the largest plates and bowls in the village. Mr. Zhu was prescient. The skin of the braised pork was as thick as cowhide, and each piece had black hairs sticking up like angry bristles. I watched carefully how the little brother would deal with it. I guessed that he liked to eat braised pork. If he were at home, he would surely be straightforward and politely use chopsticks to pick up a piece, put the junction of meat and skin between his front teeth, take a bite, and place the hairy skin on the table, and then leisurely chew the delicious meat. He certainly can't do this so happily tonight. He either won't eat it, or he will swallow it whole with the skin and hair. He is considering. After all, he made up his mind, picked up a piece, and blinked his eyes and sent it into his mouth.

First, we discussed what day to start school.

Students in the countryside always have to go to the school after February 2nd. Those who have already started learning can start earlier. But no matter what, you have to pick a good day. Of course, the official calendar is our only guide. Brother Chunsheng brought an official calendar and asked Mr. Zhu to pick a day. Mr. Zhu chose March 15th of the Gregorian calendar, which is February 9th of the lunar calendar. Brother Zhao Xiaoer said, "Let me see." Secretary Li said, "You don't know how to read, and the characters don't recognize you, so how can you tell if the day is good or bad." Brother Xiaoer said, "Xianggua looks at the official calendar, and a good day is a good day to the end. The day Mr. Zhu picked is excellent."

The First Wonder Woman in the Swimming World 117

The Success Story of Ms. Helen Madison (3) Huai Qing

▲ Effort and Success

Although Ms. Helen's new world record in 1928 was not officially recognized, it demonstrated her amazing swimming skills. The first time she became famous was during practice when she unofficially set a new world record in the 100-meter race. This was the first time that Helen Madison's name spread to the sports news columns of newspapers around the world.

Helen and her coach respected each other very much. Mr. Dodd carefully guided her technique, and Ms. Helen also humbly accepted Mr. Dodd's guidance.

Mr. Dodd said very modestly: "Ms. Helen's success is not due to my guidance. She is a naturally gifted swimmer. In my 18 years as a swimming instructor, I have never seen anyone as respectful and attentive to her own skills as Ms. Helen."

"Several years ago, when she was just a child, she already had the full ability to develop her swimming. She studied swimming intently and worked hard to improve her skills."

Before she expects to break a record, she must stipulate a practice method. For example, for a 1,000-yard swim, she first finds out how long the pool is and how many turns she needs to make. After this problem is solved, she calculates how much speed to use from the first turn to the last round trip. Ms. Helen has done a lot of research on this point, and her time and speed are very well controlled. If she wants to break this record, she makes up her mind to study and practice three or four weeks in advance.

▲ Daily Life and Diet

Swimming is very much related to food. Indigestion will affect technique. Ms. Helen is very particular about eating and training times. She believes that the following points are important for swimmers to pay attention to: (1) Eat foods that are beneficial to the body according to your appetite, eat as much as you want, but not too much.

(2) Set training times.

(3) The movements should be natural and rhythmic, not hurried.

(4) Pay attention to rest and do not overwork.

Helen said, "I practice swimming for one hour each time, three times a week. If there is a competition, I stop practicing. If I gain weight, I do other kinds of work to try to restore it to its original state."

She goes to bed at 8 or 9 o'clock every night and gets up very early in the morning. For breakfast, she chooses foods rich in nutrients, such as eggs, fruits, beef, and grains. If there is a formal competition in the afternoon, she stops exercising in the morning. After breakfast, she does some slight activity to increase her physical strength. For lunch, she eats beef and solid grains. After the meal, she rests completely. If the competition is at night, she eats at 4:30 p.m., eating beef, vegetables, biscuits, cakes, and other things. Before the competition, she does not eat anything at all.

▲ Almost Nineteen Years Old

We know that Ms. Helen's success is indeed incomparable to ordinary women or men. She is a good model for athletes. She is now five feet ten inches tall and weighs one hundred and fifty-three pounds. This is the healthy and beautiful physique that swimming has given her. She will be nineteen years old on June 19th this year.

Ms. Helen Madison in the swimming world and Ms. Helen Wills (Mrs. Moody) in the tennis world are both angels in the world. Their great success has surprised women all over the world, and even the honor of the president's wife cannot match them.

Ms. Madison graduated from Lincoln High School in Seattle in June 1931. She is very interested in various sports, such as basketball, running, and tennis, but swimming is her special skill and her special hobby. Her scholarship is also very good. Her novels and art have won the praise of Seattle critics.

▲ Denies Engagement

Ms. Helen's marriage has attracted a lot of attention, but she strongly denies it. She said, "Last winter, several newspapers in New York competed to publish the news that I was engaged to someone in New York, but I myself still don't know who my fiancé is, so I want to make a special statement that I am not engaged yet."

The University of Washington is in Ms. Helen's hometown, but she did not go to university. Her future is to find a job after participating in this year's World Games, because her family is not wealthy, and her parents only gave birth to her, their precious daughter, so she wants to help her parents, or join the professional swimming world. Now many people are encouraging her to either become a swimming instructor or a professional swimmer. (The End)

Free Talk

Quotations from the 93-year-old Ma Xiangbo

[Amber Picking Up Mustard Seeds] The Origin of Old Sayings 118

— Bian Hua

Since I published the [Original Object] talk on the 9th, I have received a letter. This letter was written by my student, Cao Zhongyuan, and I think it is very valuable, so I am publishing it:

Venerable Master Xiangbo: I am writing to you respectfully. For more than ten years, I have specialized in radio science. Last year, I returned to China from Europe and engaged in the manufacture of radio transceivers. In my daily reading, I only knew that the magnet was invented by the Yellow Emperor and electricity was created by Westerners. When I traveled to England the year before last, I bought a book by Ellison Hawks F·R·A·S· entitled Pioneers of Wireless in a bookstore in London. It also attributed the credit for magnetism to the Yellow Emperor. As for electricity, on page 10, it has the following record:

Kuopho, a Chinese physicist, wrote in the 4th century: ... yrsyy...raction of a Magnet for icon is like that of amber for the smallest grain of mustard seed. It is like a breath of wind which mysteriously penetrates through bcthand Communivsyrdiydrlgeiyhtherapidityofanarrow

According to the text, Guo Pu was a figure in the Eastern Jin Dynasty, and the date is correct. However, the original text is from which book, there is no way to verify. Some say that [Bai Kong Liu Tie] has this record, but it was not written by Guo, nor is there such a saying. Before 128, I went to the Oriental Library to browse Guo's books, but none were available. Recently, I read the Original Object article in today's Shen Bao Free Talk.

The Master said: [Amber Picking Up Mustard Seeds] was discovered as early as the Han Dynasty, which is even before Guo Pu. Although this matter is small, it is quite related to academic culture.

The Master has read extensively and must know the origin and book title of the old saying [Amber Picking Up Mustard Seeds]. I sincerely ask you to reveal the source of this ancient saying to dispel my doubts. I am extremely grateful. Respectfully yours,

Cao Zhongyuan, a student of Fudan Public School in Wusong at the end of the Xuantong period.

June 9, 21st year

Wonderful Words to Encourage the Purchase of Homespun Cloth 119

— Sun Choucheng

Since the January 28th Shanghai Incident, not only has the prosperity of the city been affected, but also the lives of rural people have been greatly impacted. In the villages under the jurisdiction of Shanghai County, rural women still spin and weave homespun cloth to maintain their families during their spare time from farming. Recently, due to the extreme tightness of money, cloth shops in the surrounding villages have had trouble with their cash flow and lack money to go to the villages to buy. This has led to the situation where the cloth woven by rural women has no one to care for it, and it is almost as if they are sitting and waiting for death. Zhang Yi, the director of the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center, in view of this situation, initiated a homespun cloth exhibition to promote it. It is scheduled for twenty days and will tour various places. Starting from the 13th of this month, it will be publicly exhibited in the Penglai Market in Nanshi for three days. Choucheng visited on the last day. There were no less than a hundred kinds of cloth on display. The patterns were mostly willow branches, squares, reed mats, and dice blocks. Although the quality is rough, it is very durable. In order to gather ideas and prepare for improvement, the association has prepared an opinion box. All the public who visit can directly state their opinions and put them in this box. Each time they arrive at a place, they will organize the opinions of the visitors and use them as reference materials. After the meeting, they will discuss them in order to adopt and improve them. The opinions seen on that day were mostly that the homespun cloth was too narrow, there were too many seams when making new clothes, and there were not many colors, so it was not as easy to catch the eye as foreign cloth. The quality is thick and durable, suitable for winter, but not for summer. It is recommended to widen the width, dye the colors so they don't fade, and use fine yarn. According to the organizers of the association, this kind of opinion is very valuable. They plan to adopt them in order and tell the farmers. Shi She, the director of the Shanghai County Education Bureau, said something very funny when reporting the motivation of this meeting. He said that the concessions in Shanghai are called "foreign fields" by the villagers. People who live in foreign fields often consider it fashionable to live in foreign houses, wear foreign clothes, speak foreign languages, and read foreign books. They regard the homespun cloth woven by the villagers as "rustic and unsophisticated," used by "country bumpkins and rustics." They don't bother to buy and use foreign goods and send foreign money to foreign countries, allowing foreigners to manufacture guns and cannons to invade China. In the eyes of foreigners, they are considered "easy targets" and not worth it. He hopes that fellow countrymen who love to use foreign goods will change their minds and buy domestic goods, and not think that they are complacent in being infected with foreign airs. Everyone laughed. Jiang Yanqiu, the chairman of the Shanghai County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee, compared foreign cloth to modern women and homespun cloth to country girls. He said that although modern women look good, they may be poisonous, and you will suffer for the rest of your life after marrying them. The proverb says that country girls "have food but no looks," which is very practical. Everyone sighed that his metaphor was accurate and applauded.

A Morbid Society 120

— Qian Taisheng

In the statistics published in this newspaper on June 6th, let's look at the statistics on suicide and divorce: there were a total of 57 suicides, the most common cause being "family incidents," accounting for 17, followed by economic oppression, accounting for 14, and the remaining falling, unemployment, and quarrels accounting for 26. We believe that the occurrence of an incident must have a major cause, and from a "sociological" point of view, it is a matter worthy of study. We must not say that they were haunted by ghosts when we saw people "die." We should believe that under what kind of social organization is that kind of phenomenon inevitable? This is definitely not something that can be summed up in one sentence. What kind of "incident" is a so-called "family incident?" This statistical table naturally does not tell us, but we can imagine that there are 17 people who are using their various methods to find "death," which is definitely not a coincidence or a case of mental disorder. That is our, our society, should bear the greatest responsibility. As for finding death because of "economic oppression," that is not surprising given the current economic organization. Look, in which country (except for Soviet Russia) are there not many people starving and waiting to die? In this day and age, not starving and not looking for death, that's too dreamy, isn't it?

As for divorce, there were a total of 43 cases, and "incompatibility" accounted for 34, with the remaining accounting for 6. We naturally have to doubt the reason for this "incompatibility." Do you think that women who let their hair down and make a fuss are simply due to the two words "incompatibility?" They, I believe, have definitely buried all the difficult-to-solve disputes and put them on the four words "incompatibility." That only shows that they have found the most simple and dignified excuse for resolving the divorce.

Naturally, we say again, if ordinary people can not solve a certain satisfaction rooted seed when they are getting married because of their own blood spurting, what other way is there but to not look for a lawyer when everything is "exposed?"

However, a morbid society is always a morbid society. Kidnappings, assassinations, and robberies are not happening in our world every day? What do you want to say? The fundamental society to be created is such a society, don't you believe it?

What I Heard About A Marriage to Laugh and Cry 121

— Ji Hui

I remember the huge cover pages of Shen Xin Liang Bao last autumn. Carrying the two film companies, Star and Great China, vying for the film adaptation rights of the novel [A Marriage to Laugh and Cry] by Zhang Henshui. The splendid and grand articles were endless. Whether they were familiar with the truth or not, the readers already knew it very well. Although half a year has passed, it is still not difficult to remember. However, there must be many who want to know the inside story. I will describe it as follows, based on what I have seen and heard.

▲ The novel has been published in Xinwen Bao's Happy Forest on a daily basis.

A Visit to a Soviet Russian Kindergarten 122

— Special

One day I (a reporter for the London Observer) visited a kindergarten in Moscow called the [Communist International]. It belongs to the workers of the clothing factory. There are about sixty children in the garden, aged between three and seven. Half of the expenses are borne by the factory. The parents only provide the children's food expenses. They eat bread, vegetables, and milk every day, plus some butter and sugar. Sometimes they eat apples. Every two or three days, they eat meat once. The facilities in the garden are among the best in Moscow. Many of the characteristics are very similar to kindergartens in other countries. The children are divided into several groups according to age. Every day, they play, read, and rest, all according to a very orderly timetable. They sculpt and cut paper to make pictures, build houses with small wooden blocks, and take care of flowers and plants. The older children have to manage things like meals. The three major things that the [Communist International] pays attention to are: devout belief in Leninism, active anti-religious propaganda, and emphasis on military toys and games. In one room, there is a wooden board hanging high. It was made by the children themselves. On it are written the words "How We Fulfill Lenin's Creed." Their methods of fulfilling the creed are different. Some donate money to Mopao (this is an organization to rescue imprisoned communists in other countries), some donate money to make airplanes, and some give toys to a "group." A proud little child boasted that he had removed the idol from his home. There is a rough drawing depicting the scene of removing the idol. Below it is a line of words saying. [There is no God. We don't want Jesus. We want to make our parents not believe in God either.] I asked a seven-year-old child standing next to me to explain the meaning of the painting. He said with a serious face. [There is no God. So we removed the idol. Only priests and capitalists say there is a God. Because they are the enemies of the workers and want to enslave the workers.] Then two more children came and said. [Of course there is no God. Children of foreign workers are not allowed to go to school. Because they are afraid that they will know that there is no God.] I then asked. [Do foreign children go to school?] This question stumped them. One of the children answered. [Some go to school. Some don't.] Another answered. [Rich children go.] I also saw portraits of Military Commissar Voroshilov and General Budyonny hanging on the wall. There were also many pictures of the army and navy fighting. The slightly taller group were all children aged six or seven. Their toys were all miniature war items. There were small tanks, small cannons, small rifles, small machine guns, and small armored trains on the table. There were also many wooden cannons on the floor, all made by the children themselves. Several children were running around the room with small rifles, pretending to shoot each other. I then asked a female teacher why she made the children pay so much attention to military supplies. She replied. [We are not peace activists. We usually tell the children in detail about the content of the Red Army. Teach them to love soldiers. When they grow up, they all want to be soldiers. We often take the children to visit the Red Army schools and barracks. Soldiers often come to us to play games with the children. We know that we will definitely be attacked by capitalist countries in the future. So we are always preparing for war. Only in this way can we fulfill Lenin's Creed.] When she said this, she also made an expressive gesture towards the Creed board on the wall. After I visited, I was left with a very deep impression, especially on the fact that military concepts are instilled in children from the very beginning.

Readers have praised it unanimously. Since Han Qiu passed away, the literary world has been silent for a long time. Getting this work with both literary and emotional beauty can be widely praised both near and far. When the whole book was finished, Sanyou Bookstore first contacted Henshui and purchased the copyright to publish it as a separate book. The sales volume was exceptionally high, setting a record. I happened to hear Li, the manager of Sanyou, tell me that it has been reprinted again and again. It has now been published in five editions. The total number of copies sold is more than 15,000, which can be said to be an unprecedented feat since the advent of social novels.

▲ The film company, Star, the manager Zhang Shichuan. With a clear mind. Since seeing the book published in Happy Forest, he immediately discussed it with Yan Duhuo and purchased the film adaptation rights from Henshui. After the contract was signed, he asked Yan to write the screenplay, the acts, and the description, all by hand. Yan is the chief priest of the literary world and a veteran craftsman. The adaptation is excellent. Star started filming last summer. They first made costumes and planned the scenery. They carefully considered it before starting. At that time, Star Company had spent 600,000 gold to buy a new sound and color camera. When this drama started filming, they went to Beiping to take real scenes. When the Shenyang Incident happened, the location work was just finished. They rushed back to make indoor scenes. They encountered obstacles and difficulties. It was finally completed last time. The film is more than 60,000 feet long. Two-tenths of it is with sound and two-tenths of it is with color. The rest is still a silent film. It is divided into six episodes. Sound and color are interspersed, creating a new style. The director Zhang imitated the Western film. I recently heard that he has signed a contract with the Nanjing Grand Theater. Today (the 19th), he will first invite people from all walks of life to preview the film. In less than a week, it will be officially released. The mega-hit film that everyone has been looking forward to will not be difficult to see at this time.

▲ Zhou Jianyun, director of the special issue distribution department of Star, and Yao Sufeng, editor of Min Bao, jointly edited the special issue of the film "A Marriage to Laugh and Cry." The preparation took five months. They have collected dozens of works from literary giants at home and abroad and printed more than 100 stills from the whole play into a huge volume using photogravure. The colors are bright and the editing is novel. It is an unprecedented work among film special issues. A total of 100,000 copies were printed. It will be released on the same day as the film is released. The audience who is fascinated by the beauty of the female stars and loves to watch the film will compete to buy it.

Records of Military Life in Shuanglou (83) 123

— Seeking a Happy Master

Chapter Ten: Powerful Families Abuse Principles, but Kind Women Offer Comfort; Shortcuts and Bribes Lead to Success, and Mountain Bandits are Enlisted into the Military.

Councilor An had no idea. He thought I had already handled everything properly at the yamen. I went there once yesterday and realized the situation wasn't right. Only then did I realize that I had forgotten to send the gift. I can only blame myself for being negligent. It's not like I'm completely clueless. Let's just send a little more to make up for it. Originally, I wanted to put together four hundred yuan in a package, which would be presentable. You can go and tell Chief Wan plainly that Councilor An hasn't gotten a good position yet. I'm sorry, but this is all we can offer for now. If we get support from everyone in the future and there are better opportunities, we certainly won't forget them. Neither Councilor An nor I are people who would let our friends down. Mao Deshun said, "Alright. What could go wrong? I'll be right back. You two wait for my news." After Mao Shun left, in less than two hours, he returned in the car they had provided. He excitedly told the couple, "Everything is settled. Wan Jinsheng accepted the money and was very polite. He said that what happened yesterday was because he didn't know. If he had known it was you two, he definitely wouldn't have acted that way, even without talking about it. Now, the Marshal is about to receive guests, and Chief Wan is eager to meet Councilor An. Why don't I accompany Councilor An there now?" As they were leaving and getting into the car, she again earnestly instructed An Yutian that when he saw Old Ye today, he must present the memorial he had prepared earlier regarding the enlistment of the bandit army and ask him to approve it immediately. Fifth Mistress has also been urging him on your behalf, so there's an eighty or ninety percent chance it will be very effective. An Yutian remembered everything well and hurriedly went with Mao Deshun to that place that was like a dragon's pool and a tiger's den. However, this time, revisiting the old place, although it had only been half a day and a night, the situation was completely different. Mao Deshun acted as a temporary bodyguard, protecting An Yutian as he strode confidently towards the chief's office in the inner room of the reception hall. He took the liberty of lifting the door curtain and letting An Yutian step in first. He followed behind and announced loudly, "Chief Wan, Councilor An is here!" An Yutian entered and looked up, seeing that the chief's office was actually quite simple and unadorned. Several wooden plank beds were placed haphazardly on both sides. The walls were cluttered with pistols, military caps, leather boots, and military belts. In the middle was a square table with a large teapot, a set of ebony dominoes, several large notebooks, and countless name cards of various sizes and colors scattered everywhere. It was not much different from the scene in the gatehouse of an ordinary mansion.

Imported quotations fell by 4, 5, and 6 jiao or more, so market sentiment was extremely depressed and the atmosphere was poor. Although major factories were in a difficult position and could no longer sell, small factories and domestic manufacturers were releasing supply slightly, so opening prices decreased. When the afternoon market opened, it initially seemed stable, but later, as selling households increased, prices for each month fell again. The reason for this decline is that actual sales are sluggish, the international atmosphere is not good, and the continued arrival of foreign wheat is likely to become a reality, so prices naturally decline, and it is not something that can be boosted in the short term. As a result, the prices for July to October each fell by 2 fen, and the price for November fell by 2 fen and 7.5 li.

The Main Reasons for the Sluggish Bidding of Wheat 134

(1) Overseas Price Decline (2) Sluggish Flour Sales (3) New Crop Season Yesterday's futures wheat market saw mostly flat and weak prices for each month. Imported wheat quotations fell by 4, 5, and 6 jiao or more, indicating that overseas surpluses remained unchanged. Domestic flour sales also remained sluggish. This is the season for new wheat, so the difficulty in raising market prices is unavoidable. However, for near-term contracts, such as July, local merchants still intend to buy, and they buy as soon as prices fall slightly, making it difficult for prices to fall too low in the short term. In the long term, the relationship with imported wheat makes market sentiment poor. As a result, prices for July, August, and September each fell by 3 fen, and the price for October fell by 4 fen, and the price for November fell by 3 fen. New wheat transactions were still not smooth, with an opening price of 85% for An Ding wheat at 2 taels and 7 qian, and Fang Tai wheat at 2 taels and 6 qian, totaling 700 bags.
