Tunchi Fine Eyebrow Tea Plummets Again 137

Since Tunchi Fine Eyebrow green tea suffered a sharp drop in price last week, the market has been exhibiting a pessimistic outlook. Various foreign firms have been hesitant to buy, fearing further price declines. This has caused extreme panic and a sluggish market. Recently, firms like Wo Ho and Kam Lung resumed trading in Tunchi Fine Eyebrow, dealing in several hundred cases, with prices dropping to ninety taels. Consequently, all types of green tea, including Fine Eyebrow and Needle Eyebrow, are declining in unison, creating a dire situation. According to well-informed sources, only collective firmness can reverse this decline. Current stockpiles of green tea in the Moroccan market are only about three to four thousand cases, a very low level. Meanwhile, the harvests of beans and wheat in that region are abundant, indicating strong future consumption. The current sluggish market is mainly attributed to the rapid price drops in the Shanghai market.

Recent Overview of the World Silk Market 138

(Report from the Tung Foong Silk Trading Company for May of the 21st Year)

The silk market in May was severely impacted by a downward trend, leading to a sharp decline. Silk prices reached new record lows. A table is provided below:

New York Raw Silk Yokohama Raw Silk

Exchange Sayu Raw Silk Exchange

First Month Future First Month Future

Silk Silk

May 2nd 1.33 520 55.10

May 9th 1.30 490 45.00

May 17th 1.22 460 42.70

May 23rd 1.20 470 42.40

May 30th 1.11 420 35.50

After Kan Lee bought 108,000 piculs of raw silk from the Japanese government at the end of April, the silk industry generally believed that such a large quantity of spot goods, once controlled by the government and transferred into private hands, would cause a strong reaction and that the silk market might have a stable upward trend. However, the reality was not so. In the first week of May, the American Silk Association announced that American silk mills used only 35,799 piculs of silk in April (46,761 piculs in March 1932, 41,356 piculs in April 1931). The silk market started to decline again because Japanese silk exporters were frantically dumping new silk in New York at extremely low prices (for example, Mitsui sold new silk of 20/22 denier with 85-point evenness at US$1.20 per pound (equivalent to 460 taels of silver at an exchange rate of US$31.50), and 20/22 denier with 83-point evenness at US$1.10 per pound (equivalent to 415 taels of silver at an exchange rate of US$31.50). This intensified the downward trend, coupled with the fact that new silk was approaching the market, which usually caused the market to show signs of decline. Therefore, there was no possibility of an upward trend.

Economic recession and the decline of various industries are another reason for the low silk prices. Taking the United States as an example, not only is there no progress, but it is also becoming increasingly tired. In this time of worldwide depression, the US government has found it difficult to maintain its fiscal budget, and the legislature is still continuing various new plans, with debates over various new bills, the struggle between expansion and contraction, which has not been resolved so far. This phenomenon only increases instability and chaos at home and abroad. As a result, businesses are cautious and have to reduce their business scope to a minimum, which is also natural. As for the current situation of the American silk industry, the silk weaving industry is more favorable. With inventories running out, factories may increase production again. In the hosiery industry, due to sluggish sales, there is also little profit. However, due to the low price of natural silk, it has fierce competition with rayon. If used for weaving cheap clothing or shirts, etc., it can almost replace rayon. Therefore, the rayon industry has been greatly affected. It is heard that several factories will temporarily close part of their work in June, and reopen when the price of natural silk is slightly higher and competition can be avoided.

The Lyon exchange in May was cleared and the prices were slightly lower, which was entirely manipulated by speculators. The extent of speculation by these short sellers can be illustrated by the following example. Buyers here wanted to buy factory brand 13/22 factory silk, offering 750 taels, but the factory was still unwilling to sell. However, in Lyon, someone was willing to sell it for 100 francs (equivalent to 650 taels of silver) (speculators are bearish on the market, so they sell first, and then buy back when the price falls).

At the end of May, silk such as San Tiao Wu Heng Jin (HY) and Yue Tu brand could be sold for 95 to 97 francs, but by the end of the month, these silks could only be sold for 80 to 82 francs. Tung Foong had a telegram saying that Yue Tu or San Tiao Wu ungraded silk was quoted as low as 71 francs (equivalent to 480 taels of silver).

Europe's hope for increasing silk sales is still very slim. One reason is that the European political situation is not optimistic. In particular, the German National Socialist Party has recently gained momentum, and there are fears of more political disputes in the future. Secondly, the Danube countries are practically on the verge of bankruptcy, and their economic crisis needs to be resolved urgently. The British government recently added another 20% to the existing import tax on silk fabrics, causing great panic in the Lyon and Zurich markets in Switzerland. The exports of these two places all rely on sales to the United Kingdom. As far as the raw silk market is concerned, the decline in exports to the United Kingdom has reduced exports, while on the other hand, British production will definitely increase. Since the pound fell in value, the sales of raw silk in the United Kingdom have improved slightly this year.

All the important reasons driving down silk prices at present have been listed above. However, from another perspective, the current situation is not as bleak as people generally think. Why? Because in the current economic panic, the prices of various raw materials are also falling, but raw silk is worse. However, the raw silk inventory in various places, including the silk that the Japanese government is preparing to export, is not enough for four months, even at the current lowest consumption rate. Although new silk will be on the market in a few months, its output is greatly reduced compared to last year, so the silk market will not decline because of it. On the contrary, the domestic silk sales volume will not only not decrease, but also have a great hope of starting to increase as autumn approaches. We can be optimistic about the harmony between the supply and demand of raw silk in the coming season.

The daily drop in silk prices makes silkworm farmers unprofitable, so the cocoon output decreased greatly last year, and it is feared that it will be even shorter this year.

Although the French silkworm industry was subsidized by the government last year, if calculated based on the total cocoon output of the country, it has decreased by 60%. The cocoon output in Italy decreased by about 30% last year. This year, the government is strongly encouraging the public to love their motherland and raise more silkworms, but as a result, the output is afraid that it will be reduced even more. Farmers in several places have even cut down mulberry trees. This year's spring cocoons in Japan are about 8% less than last year. Due to the high cost of fertilizer and the poverty of farmers, the mulberry leaves are not good. Even if the weather has no special changes, the output and quality of new cocoons will definitely not be very good. This year, the spring cocoon industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang has already started weighing, the quality is very poor, and the output is about 50% to 60% less than last year. We must keep in mind that this economic crisis, no matter what its initial cause is, is not so much a credit failure as a lack of self-confidence. No matter what kind of goods, no matter how strong their statistical position is, unless the world's economic and political situation changes to the point where credit is fully restored, it is difficult for the goods to fully recover from the current decline. The quantity of raw silk shipped to American factories is attached below:

This year Last year March 46761 55383

January 58793 55910 April 35199 41356

The American silk inventory is attached again as follows:

The general situation of the silk industry is as described above. Recently, the Ministry of Industry, together with the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provincial Governments, at the request of silk merchants, decided to exempt all taxes on the export of raw silk, and first issued treasury bonds of 2.2 million taels to subsidize the export of old silk at 100 taels per picul. Two committees for rectification and promotion were also organized to complete it. The government has done its best to rescue the silk industry, but the silk price is falling, and the dispute between the factory and the silver money industry cannot be resolved immediately. Although domestic silk factories do not buy much silk, the price is still better. However, foreign sales are still difficult. Apart from a few transactions by French firms in the monthly digest, there is no development by American firms. Therefore, to solve the problem of domestic silk inventory, it is hoped that the factory and the silver money industry will understand each other as soon as possible. If the world situation changes slightly, the silk price will immediately improve.

▲Opening Speech Chairman Wang Xiaolai delivered the opening speech at the third member representative assembly, saying, "Distinguished guests, representatives, today, this association is convened by the executive committee in accordance with Article 39, Paragraph 1 of Chapter 7 of the association's constitution, which states that the members' assembly is held regularly in mid-June every year, and Article 24 of Chapter 5, which states that the term of office of the executive committee and the supervisory committee is four years, and half of the members are re-elected every two years, and those who should be re-elected may not be re-elected, but the first re-election is determined by drawing lots. Eight executive committee members and four supervisory committee members of the first session will remain in office, and will be alternately re-elected thereafter. Candidate executive and supervisory committee members will be re-elected in full every two years, and those who are re-elected may be re-elected. After discussing the various regulations, the 92nd standing committee meeting submitted them to the 24th executive committee meeting for resolution, and convened the third member representative assembly today to discuss the proposals submitted by the members and this association, and legally held the first re-election. This is the process of convening this session of the conference in accordance with legal procedures, and it is necessary to declare it first. Today, a total of 156 members of the trade association and 30 members of the store members attended, for a total of 326 representatives, and we are honored that the competent authorities have sent personnel to attend and provide guidance, and we must express our honor. As for the situation in which this association has been in the past year, it can be said that most of the time it has been trying to cope in crisis, suspicion, shock, anxiety, and distress, so as to avoid failure. I dare to comfort myself in private, and I am barely enough to live up to the heavy trust of all members. I have selected the most important tasks of this association in this session, and I would like to present them to the conference. (1) The course of dealing with the violent takeover by the Shanghai Special Municipality Merchant [Sports Committee]. At the beginning of the Ningyue cooperation last year, the so-called Shanghai Special Municipality Merchant Sports Committee suddenly appeared in this city, and its stated goal was to unify the Shanghai merchant groups. On the afternoon of November 18 last year, the committee led dozens of plainclothes people in trucks to the meeting with a fierce momentum. The leader claimed in public that he was ordered to take over, so he sent people to guard the offices of each department, the telephone switchboard, and each branch, and monitored them uniformly. This association, seeing that the matter was extraordinary, immediately convened an emergency meeting of the standing committee and resolved to petition the municipal government to send police to the meeting to maintain order, and Chairman Wang personally went to the meeting to meet with the personnel who were violently taking over and asked them who ordered them to take over, and they could not answer. Therefore, the plainclothes people were first expelled, and then sternly refuted and refused to hand over on the spot. The personnel who took over returned disappointedly. This association also believes that the committee's remarks published in the newspaper were enough to confuse the world's hearing, so this association was reorganized by the Chamber of Commerce and Industry Association, and the Chamber of Commerce and Industry Association was ordered by the Central Political Conference to merge the four former merchant groups within a time limit. After the reorganization was completed, it was officially produced in accordance with the new Chamber of Commerce Law, and the Chamber of Commerce Law was drafted, reviewed and passed by the Legislative Yuan. All the processes were clearly stated and submitted to the government, the court, and the competent authorities for legal correction, and all the executive and supervisory committee members issued a declaration to dispel the world's doubts and correct the vision of merchants and people. As a result, the Shanghai Municipal Government soon received an order from the central government to close the association, and this association was not illegally robbed. This is something that can be gratifying. (2) Regarding the Northeast Incident and the efforts to cope with the Shanghai War, since September 18 last year, the Japanese army invaded Shenyang with lightning speed and occupied the three provinces of Liaojihei in a few days. After hearing the news, this association, on the one hand, the members participated in the city's Anti-Japanese Association and worked hard, and on the other hand, repeatedly sent secret telegrams to the central government and Zhang's Appeasement Director, outlining the opinions on sending troops to rescue. Although Zhang's Appeasement Director replied by telegram that he would adopt them, he was never able to put them into practice. To this day, Shan Hei Shui is still slaughtered under the iron hooves of the Japanese army, which is painful to say. Because the Eastern Province did not resist, the violent Japanese saw China as uninhabited, and dispatched a large number of naval landing forces, and the joint fleet came to Shanghai. On the day when the municipal authorities satisfactorily answered the request, they suddenly sent troops to attack Zhabei on the night of January 28. The 19th Route Army stationed in Songhu fought bloody battles with the 5th Army to defend the country and repeatedly defeated the enemy's attack. The Japanese soldiers were discouraged, so they flew to Tokyo to transfer reinforcements, iron warships, and planes came one after another. This association believes that Songhu is an important town in the southeast, guarding the capital. If it is lost, it will affect the overall situation. It has repeatedly telegraphed the central government and the Military Commission, Chairman Chiang, and the commander-in-chief, etc., to transfer troops to rescue the situation day and night in order to ensure all-round safety. In the end, it was too late to help, and there was a general retreat of the enemy soldiers on March 2. When I think about it today, there is still pain. At the beginning of the incident, this association was in a leading position of merchants and was forced by this disaster, so it had to express something. Therefore, it immediately notified all merchants in the city to go on strike for three days to jointly resist the invaders. On the one hand, the soldiers on the front line were fighting hard against the enemy, and the goods needed for military affairs and the application of materials must be continuously supplied so that they could do their best to fight. Therefore, a donation office for relief and condolence goods was organized, and funds were raised separately. In the early stage, this association sent letters to chambers of commerce and commercial organizations in various places, sincerely soliciting donations. Therefore, the number of donations and goods sent from various places was not small. The accounts have now been announced in order to show credibility. When the League of Nations investigation team came to Shanghai, this association believed that the members of the team were entrusted by the League of Nations General Assembly to come to China, and they were responsible for a very important mission. Therefore, at the reception, the cause of the Northeast Incident and the right and wrong of all disputes between Japan and China, which the Japanese army disregarded world peace and justice, were carefully presented to the members of the investigation team, which aroused international attention. (4) Member Requests to Withdraw. Resolved: (A) The Science Instrument Museum's request to withdraw is not approved. (B) The Gold Industry Exchange's request to withdraw is not approved. (C) The Tianyiwei Mother Factory's request to withdraw should be handled with gentle persuasion by the Executive Committee. (D) The Sichuan Store's request to withdraw is not approved. (5) The Renewal Stage's request to withdraw is approved. (6) The association's income and expenditure settlement for the 20th year and the income and expenditure budget proposal for the 21st year are resolved and passed. (7) The settlement for the 20th year and the budget for the 21st year show a total deficit of 50,077.96 yuan. How to raise funds? Resolved: The Executive and Supervisory Committee members will explore new sources of revenue and reduce expenditures. (8) Issue a declaration opposing the establishment of a free city in Shanghai. Resolved: Passed. (9) Petition the government to demand that Japan compensate for the losses of the Shanghai war. Resolved: Passed. (10) Petition the government to provide relief to various industries due to the losses of the Shanghai war. Resolved: Petition the government to promptly develop relief measures for the industrial and commercial sectors in the Songhu war zone and implement them immediately. (11) All industry associations and firms should join industry associations, and industry associations should join the Chamber of Commerce, in accordance with legal principles, to establish a unified and consolidated organizational foundation. Resolved: Passed. Petition the Legislative Yuan to amend the Industry Association Law. Before the Industry Association Law is amended, request the Ministry of Industry of the Executive Yuan to provide relief by issuing a ministerial order, and the Executive Committee will send representatives to Beijing to petition. (12) Petition the government to plan a unified system of weights and measures, which should be implemented simultaneously nationwide to avoid obstacles. Resolved: Petition the government to implement it simultaneously nationwide to avoid obstacles. (13) Discuss the special business tax of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, which merchants and citizens cannot bear. Please unite all chambers of commerce in the province to oppose it and strive to achieve the purpose of abolishing it. Resolved: Submit to the Executive Yuan. All disguised likin, regardless of what name they are levied under, should be strictly prohibited. (14) Discuss the petition to the government to properly formulate measures to save domestic silk. The detailed measures will be handed over to the Executive Committee to convene relevant industries to discuss opinions and submit them to the government for adoption and implementation. ▲Outgoing Committee Members: The terms of the following committee members have expired: (1) Seven Executive Committee members: Fang Jiaobo, Gu Xinyi, Pei Yunqing, Xu Jiqing, Yuan Deng, Wu Zhihao, Zhang Peizhen. (2) Three Supervisory Committee members: Ma Jiliang, Cheng Bianchun, Lu Qisheng.

▲Elected Committee Members: (A) Executive Committee: (1) Chen Zheqing, 119 votes; (2) Guo Nan, 118 votes; (3) Ma Shaoquan, 113 votes; (4) Pan Shengsheng, 112 votes; (5) Yu Zuoting, 91 votes; (6) Chen Xiangzhou, 91 votes; (7) Ma Jiliang, 24 votes. (C) Alternate Executive Committee members: (1) Ye Jiaxing, 90 votes; (2) Xie Zhongle, 78 votes; (3) Shao Baoxing, 71 votes; (4) Zhang Peizhen, 65 votes; (5) Chen Liangyu, 30 votes; (6) Gu Jiuru, 25 votes; (7) Wang Yunwu, 8 votes. (D) Alternate Supervisory Committee members: (1) Zhang Yichen, 65 votes; (2) Chen Ziming, 51 votes; (3) Wang Bofen, 47 votes.

▲Closing Remarks: The closing remarks of the members' meeting stated: "The association has only been established for two years. The year from the closing of the second session to the closing of the third session can be said to be one of the most difficult years. Not only has the economy suffered significant losses due to the Shanghai war, but the handling of affairs has also been unprecedentedly difficult. Originally, popular organizations take the social environment as their environment and the national environment as their environment. Since the country has encountered extraordinary changes and the merchants and citizens of the city have suffered a tragedy unprecedented in a century, the pain and suffering of the association in handling affairs are self-evident. What the members of the association regret most is that although they have worked day and night for the past year, without even a moment of rest, they have not made much contribution to alleviating the suffering of merchants and citizens, and they must take the blame in public. Fortunately, after the re-election, the newly elected gentlemen are all rich in knowledge and talent and will surely show new initiatives and make up for the shortcomings of the past. The purpose of this session in handling affairs is to strive for the abolition of internal warfare and the promotion of domestic goods. This matter is not only to find a way out for merchants and citizens, but also to find a way out for the country. With the Shanghai incident initially resolved, handling affairs after this may be a little smoother compared to the previous session, but the complexity of the progress and the importance of the responsibility may be ten or a hundred times greater than the previous session. In fact, these two matters may seem like clichés, but to achieve practical results, it all depends on persistence and perseverance, and doing it practically. Therefore, after the closing of this session of the assembly, it is the beginning of the association's major work. We would like to offer our encouragement and hope today."

▲Declarations Issued: Based on the resolutions of the general meeting, the following declarations were issued: (1) This year, the association's work should focus on abolishing internal warfare and promoting domestic goods. The Taishi Gong Biography of Merchants and Colonization states: "Agriculture produces it, industry creates it, and commerce circulates it." Therefore, agriculture and industry are the foundation of commerce. In the world, no country has merchants thriving and prospering while its rural areas are bankrupt and its industries are withering. Since China opened its ports, it has competed in the market with mechanized and scientific industries using its own closed-door handicraft industries. Like pouring soup on snow, it has suffered defeat after defeat. Therefore, the so-called wealthy merchants and big businesses of the past have all been eliminated. Those who pursue the small profits in the market have only imported goods as their means of survival, sharing the crumbs left over from foreign merchants. Therefore, those who hold opinions often say that in recent decades, China has had no commerce to speak of. The so-called merchants are merely the agents of foreign merchants. Think about it, the trade deficit increases year by year. Last year, the trade deficit even reached a staggering 500 million. How can we deny this kind of sarcastic but truly painful statement? Fellow merchants, with blood and knowledge, and patriotic thoughts, would they be willing to remain as agents of foreign merchants for a long time? I know they will surely be heartbroken and swear to deny it. Moreover, taking a step back, based on the current situation, even if they want to remain agents of foreign merchants for a long time, is it allowed by the facts? For twenty years, as a result of cyclical internal warfare, the phenomenon of many soldiers, many bandits, and many starving people has been created. Let us look at the Yangtze River basin, the Huai River basin, and the Yellow River basin, all of which were once known as wealthy and prosperous regions and markets for sales. What do they have now? Those who travel among them only see armed comrades who are half-fed, groups of bandits with fierce faces, and starving people with emaciated bodies waiting for death in the market. Even if fellow merchants have the skills to dance with long sleeves and are good at accumulating wealth, the vast majority of the common people, 99% of the country, are busy saving themselves from death, and how can they have the resources to absorb excess goods? Therefore, in view of the above situation, the association believes that the association's mission from now on must be to focus on abolishing internal warfare and promoting domestic goods to find a way out for merchants. No matter how great the resistance, the goal will remain unchanged. The reason for the current turmoil and frequent wars is that talented people want to seek material enjoyment. They either go north to the barbarians or south to Yue, engaging in political maneuvering and causing the world to disintegrate, so that they can never achieve their great desires. In short, the reason why internal warfare in our country does not cease can almost be said to be driven by a few people who want to achieve their material desires. These few people, unfortunately, are in a society where agriculture is collapsing, and they recklessly admire the consumption of industrially advanced countries, causing scholars to be uneasy as scholars and the masses to flock to the path of taking risks and seeking luck. If we can promote domestic goods as a stepping stone to revitalize industry, then all the talented people in the country will be able to gather their talents and work within the system, each using their strengths to serve society, without having to pursue wild ambitions and harm the country. Even the majority of unemployed civilians will be able to resume their old occupations without having to enlist in the army. This is especially related to the abolition of internal warfare, and those who have the ambition to conquer our country will also be able to promote the collapse of their industry, so that they may one day have a sudden realization and return our invaded land and complete our golden bowl, which may be possible to achieve. The responsibility is great, and it lies entirely on the shoulders of our merchants. We respectfully state this purpose as a replacement for words of peace." (2) Declaration opposing the establishment of a free city in Shanghai: "Since Japan occupied Shenyang on September 18 last year, it has used its military force to annex Jilin and Heilongjiang, support puppets, and plan to place the three northeastern provinces under a disguised Japanese territory. The Nine-Power Treaty of Washington, which it signed itself, has long been regarded as废纸. Therefore, recently, important figures in that country have repeatedly expressed their intention to revise the treaty, knowing full well that the United States has made a stern statement in advance, and that other friendly nations may not necessarily echo it. Therefore, they are using a two-pronged approach, first trying to involve friendly nations in the Yangtze River basin to create a situation of jointly undermining the Nine-Power Treaty, so that when Japan proposes a revision of the treaty, it can hopefully achieve its goals smoothly. We cannot help but admire their ruthless methods and careful planning. What is their plan? It is the Shanghai Free City that has been making a lot of noise recently. If we analyze the Shanghai Free City proposed by the Japanese, it is nothing more than the transformation of the dictatorial South Manchuria Railway Company into a South Manchuria Railway Company with international joint organization, adding a non-Chinese, non-horse disguised independent country within the Chinese territory, so that in addition to the Manchuria country monopolized by Japan, there is also a Shanghai Free City monopolized by the international community, facing each other from afar. Then Japan's monopolization of the Northeast and the revision of the Nine-Power Treaty can be justified and not afraid of foreign refutation. Therefore, the current Shanghai Free City under consideration is different from the Manchuria country supported by Japan in terms of size and scope, but in terms of hindering China's territorial integrity and sovereignty, the nature of the two cases is equally serious and there is no difference between them. For the sake of survival and self-defense, China cannot tolerate the breaking of the Nine-Power Treaty, allowing the Japanese to sit back and enjoy the situation they have created in the three northeastern provinces. The friendly nations that convened the Washington Conference and the friendly nations that jointly signed the treaty also all regarded the treaty as a lifeline for maintaining the balance of power in the Far East and eliminating world disputes. Since the September 18th Incident, Japan has long regarded the treaty as a thorn in its side and will never want to be fooled by the Japanese again, helping them to create a situation of adding wings to a tiger. Not only that, but foreign businessmen in China have a shallower political relationship and a deeper commercial relationship, and they may not feel that there is a great need to uphold the spirit of the Nine-Power Treaty. However, the association dares to state here that foreign merchants doing business in China deeply welcome the principle of open doors, but they should know that the foundation of open doors must be built on the integrity of China's territory and sovereignty, so that the opening can be practical. Taking the current situation in the three northeastern provinces as an example, the Japanese have repeatedly stated to foreign businessmen that their doors are open, but China's territorial sovereignty has been deprived by them, and the commerce of foreign businessmen in the area has also plummeted, deeply feeling the oppression. If foreign merchants take their own interests into account, is it better to uphold the Nine-Power Treaty and respect China's sovereignty, or to help the Japanese with their mistakes and undermine China's sovereignty? Don't say that the situation in Shanghai is different from that in the three northeastern provinces. If the proposal for a free city becomes a reality, all countries can share a piece of the pie, but they should know that Japan, with its proximity, the similarity of the customs of the two peoples, and the ease of transferring factories, is easy to gain an advantage in everything. In recent years, Japan's import trade in Shanghai has been rising sharply, almost taking the top spot from the United Kingdom, and other countries are even further behind. As for the power established in the concessions, it is even more deeply rooted and growing year by year. As evidenced by the Songhu War, the Japanese military's unique freedom of movement in the concessions has almost taken the place of the painstaking efforts of the United Kingdom and the United States over the past few decades. If the Shanghai Free City is established, it will only increase Japan's power, making it a second Qingdao and a second Dalian. As the saying goes, "Gathering hundreds of flowers to make honey, for whom are you working so hard?" Why are our friendly foreign merchants still not aware of this? Therefore, the association respectfully makes the following declaration based on the resolution of the members' meeting: (1) The Japanese proposal for a Shanghai Free City is a strategy to involve friendly nations in jointly undermining the Nine-Power Treaty. The association vows to lead the merchants and citizens of the city and resolutely oppose it. (2) This proposal will surely create an opportunity for the Japanese to monopolize the Southern industry in Shanghai and weaken the commercial position of friendly nations in China. For the sake of benefiting others and ourselves, we should wake up and make the same determination to oppose it as Chinese merchants. (3) Japan has many advantages in its commerce with China, but at the same time, it also has indelible weaknesses that foreign merchants must not ignore. As a result of Japan's historical aggression against China, its relationship has been severely damaged. Therefore, the country is trying to involve foreign merchants in a vortex, so that the Chinese people will treat all countries with the same mentality as they treat Japan. This will naturally eliminate the country's commercial weaknesses. We hope that foreign merchants can see through this point and cooperate with Chinese merchants." (3) Declaration opposing the opium monopoly: "The minimum duty of a government that stands in the world is to ensure that its people have the food necessary to sustain their lives. For the past ten years, the military has forced civilians to grow opium, and this has become an open government policy. Selling opium specially and collecting special taxes has become a common plan for raising military funds. Recalling the beginning of the Republic of China, in provinces such as Hunan and Zhejiang, those who planted even a few opium seedlings in their fields were executed. The ban on opium has been relaxed and tightened, like the difference between heaven and hell, and one cannot help but feel as if they are in another world. In recent years, the Northwest has suffered severe droughts for several years in a row, and tens of thousands of people have starved to death, roughly equal to the population of a medium-sized European country, which is unprecedented in history. Even Sichuan, known as the "Land of Abundance," which used to supply other provinces with surplus grain, has recently been plagued by famine. Civilian silver and grain, and even more so the juncture of Yu and Anhui, starving people filled the roads, and people were sold in the market. There is no need to discuss the reasons for these disasters, which are due to planting poisonous weeds and uprooting good crops. There has been a lack of storage in peacetime, resulting in the people being helpless in the face of lean years. Therefore, in recent years, starving people have spread across the country, thanks to the promotion of opium cultivation by the military. To be frank, our country has long been publicly planting and selling opium, but the so-called public sale is only a semi-official public sale by local governments. However, it has already led to the current situation of starving people and bandits everywhere. Although the government has worked hard day and night, it has no way to clean up this rotten situation. If the public sale by local governments is expanded to a public sale by the central government, the whole country will fall into darkness, resulting in no qualified young men available in wartime and no sufficient food to support themselves in peacetime. In the event of repeated years of famine and an international emergency, the seaports are blocked and the import of foreign grain is cut off, what other way is there to save ourselves except to starve to death? The whole nation will not perish from foreign aggression, but from opium, which is to be expected. People and gentlemen of the country, do not say that this is an oversensitive statement by the agency. If you think about the great disaster of last year, what the starving people relied on to survive was a large amount of American wheat lent on credit. The international situation is constantly changing. Begging for food is not a long-term solution. As a result of the opium monopoly, the areas where opium is forced to be planted will inevitably expand even further than they are today. The military's reliance on opium as the lifeline for raising military funds will also become even closer. Taking the establishment of likin during the Xianfeng and Tongzhi periods as an example, once in it, the more one sinks, the deeper one gets. The authorities will inevitably drink poison willingly and enjoy it tirelessly. Therefore, in the recent facts of the new epidemic, there are even places where new water conservancy projects are being built, not encouraging people to plant rice but ordering people to plant opium. Such a retrograde act is lamented by both Chinese and foreigners. This is the phenomenon of starving people and bandits everywhere in our country today. If this state continues for another three to five years, it will not only lead to the destruction of the country and the extinction of the race. Since we have proved that the recent famine and public opium planting are causally related, then prohibiting the secret opium monopoly is a necessary requirement for the people to maintain their lives and the minimum duty of the government to protect the food supply for all. If there are fallacies such as controlling it by levying taxes to confuse the public and recklessly hope to open up a shortcut to raise funds, then this kind of strategy is only applied by the British, Dutch, and Japanese to their colonies. Even the dying Qing government at the end of the Xuantong period was unwilling to do this. If such rumors become a reality, the association will definitely follow the people of the whole country and strive to oppose it. Therefore, we publish the above declaration based on the resolution of the conference and the general meeting, and all our compatriots should take note of it."

Li Liejun's Telegram to Wang Jingwei 146

Central Committee Member Li Liejun's Telegram, Please circulate to all newspapers: I recently sent a telegram to President Wang of the Executive Yuan in Nanjing, which read: President Wang of the Executive Yuan in Nanjing, Greetings. For several months, my health has deteriorated, and I have been unable to assist in major political affairs. However, the country is declining, and the people are in turmoil. How can I not be concerned? I merely remember that during my time in the central government, my proposals to respect civil rights and implement a national political system were unlikely to be adopted. I feared that future generations would view the present as we view the past, so I remained silent. Now, reading your telegram, I understand your great aspirations to consider the people of the whole country, lamenting the pressure of foreign aggression, the destruction of our territory, and your desire to dedicate your life to national crisis for a long time. However, natural human rights are being deprived. Even when expressing opinions or writing, one may be blamed. Participating in politics and taking responsibility is even less likely. How can the people recognize the government as an organization suitable for a democratic country, or view the government's measures as embodying the spirit of democracy? Putting myself in their place, could I remain silent? If we want the entire nation to unite against foreign aggression, we must first ensure that the people have a unified way to participate in politics. Moreover, the First and Second Plenary Sessions already had resolutions to protect the people's freedom, yet they cannot be earnestly implemented. What hope can we have now? I recall that our party has been in power for several years. In the past, power was in the hands of Chiang Kai-shek, and today power rests with you, sir. The responsibility of the former was smaller, but the responsibility of the latter is truly great. Our party members often say that it is difficult to lead the nation to peace and prosperity, but in reality, the difficulty lies not in the measures, but in sincerity. The Book says, "The people can be approached, but not looked down upon." Sun Yat-sen said, "Government of the people, by the people, for the people." The affairs of the nation have reached this point, we can reverse course and plan anew. Reading the telegram has moved me, and I offer my humble opinion, hoping that you, sir, will support the precarious situation and uphold the country. Li Liejun, etc., I respectfully report, Li Liejun.

Two Railway Bureaus 148

Scheduled Memorial Service for Deceased Employees

▲ A Memorial Monument is Planned to be Built in Wusong

During the intense fighting in Shanghai, the employees of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus continued to serve at risk amidst gunfire and explosions. Some even sacrificed their lives. To comfort the dead and encourage those who came after, the Railway Bureau is preparing to hold a memorial service for the deceased employees to commemorate them. It is now scheduled to be held on the 28th of this month at the North Station. The Bureau also plans to build a memorial monument for the deceased employees in the Wusong area, where the fighting was intense. The exact location has not yet been determined. However, after the memorial service on the morning of the 28th, Director Chen will accompany the various department heads to Wusong to hold the groundbreaking ceremony for the memorial monument. Two Railway Bureaus Organize Police Department 149

▲ Officially Established on the 1st of Next Month

▲ Existing Police Affairs Section to be Abolished

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureaus previously received instructions from the Ministry of Railways to organize the Railway Ministry's Police Department stationed at the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways to manage police affairs related to the two lines. According to Mr. Ding Zhenheng, Secretary of the Railway Bureau, speaking to a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency yesterday, the Police Department will be officially established on the 1st of next month. The department is subordinate to the Police Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Railways. The current director is Ma Shaoping, who is the director of the Training Department of the Police Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Railways. After the establishment of the Police Department, the Police Affairs Section of the Railway Bureau will be abolished, and the personnel in the section will mostly serve in the Police Department.

Second Annual Conference of the Textile Society 150

▲ Held in Wuxi Today

The Chinese Textile Society is the largest group organized by textile industrialists in the country, with 374 members. The second annual conference of members this year, as decided at the last annual meeting, is being held in Wuxi. Today, the (19th), is the date of the conference. More than forty members from Shanghai left for Wuxi this morning by early train to attend the annual conference. In addition, members from Nantong, Suzhou, Changzhou, Xiaoshan, Ningbo, and other places have also gone to attend. Wuxi will have a grand welcome, and the local industrial community also attaches great importance to this conference. The proposed schedule for the two-day conference is disclosed as follows:

▲ Today's Schedule: After Shanghai members arrive in Wuxi on the first express train, all Wuxi members will welcome them at the station. They will all take cars together to visit the Lixin Textile Dyeing Factory in Huishan. After the visit, they will go to Huishan Park to attend a welcome banquet hosted by Mr. Tang Junyuan, the director of the Lixin Factory. After the meal, they will take cars to Meiyuan Park and hold a meeting in the Anboat Hall in the park. The meeting program includes discussing association affairs, re-electing officers, reading papers, etc. Dinner will be held in the park, hosted by Mr. Rong Desheng, the owner of the Shenxin Yarn Factory. If the discussion of association affairs is not completed during the day, the meeting will continue in the evening. They will stay overnight at the Taihu Hotel in the park that night.

▲ Tomorrow's Schedule: At 7:00 AM, they will take cars from Meiyuan to Xiaojishan to enjoy the morning scenery. They will then take a painted boat to Yuantouzhu, where they will have breakfast and sightseeing at the invitation of Mr. Yang Hanxi, the owner of Guangqin Yarn Factory. They will board a boat and head to Liyuan Park for sightseeing. After the sightseeing, they will board a boat for lunch, hosted by all Wuxi members. In the afternoon, they will go by boat to visit the Shenxin Third Textile Factory and the Huaxin Silk Factory. At around 6:00 PM, the boat will arrive at Gongyun Bridge. They will disembark and go to the New World Hotel for a dinner party organized by the Wuxi Textile Factory Association. At 8:00 PM, all Wuxi members will bid farewell to the members from other places at the station and part ways.

Liu Manqing's Whereabouts After Leaving Shanghai 151

Ms. Liu Manqing, a special commissioner appointed by the National Government to investigate the Kang-Tibet dispute, came to Shanghai to report everything to various sectors after going to Nanjing to meet with members of the Central Committee and report on the truth of the Kang-Tibet dispute. It is now known that after leaving Shanghai, Ms. Liu arrived in Hong Kong on the 15th of this month, changed to the Qiongzhou Wheel, entered Yunnan via Annam, and transferred to Kang-Tibet. However, according to Zhu Qiong, Ms. Liu's representative in Nanjing, some generals in Sichuan have falsely accused Ms. Liu of impersonating a commissioner and colluding with the Dalai Lama. Ms. Liu has formally submitted a request to the central government for investigation.

Various Sectors Firmly 152

Oppose Rent Concession Telephone Price Increase

▲ Organize User Federation to Cope With

Since the Rent Concession Telephone Company's price increase was approved by the Municipal Council, various groups in the city have expressed firm opposition and demanded that the Chinese directors of the Municipal Council strive to cancel it. Yesterday, the Citizens' Federation held an emergency meeting on this matter to discuss countermeasures. It was immediately decided to organize a user federation to fight the company collectively. According to a standing committee member of the City Federation speaking to a reporter from the Guomin News Agency, this telephone price increase disregards the burden on users, and the increase for shops is as high as 34.6%. In the past, it only cost 19.5 taels of silver per quarter, but now it will increase to 26.25 taels of silver. Even residential areas will increase by 25%, from 13 taels of silver to 16.25 taels of silver. The most unacceptable thing is that the new price must be calculated from March 27th of this year. When paying the telephone bill for this quarter, users must also make up for the shortfall from the previous quarter. Therefore, no matter what, users must unite and firmly oppose it until the goal of suspending the price increase is achieved.

Local News 2

All Yangtze River Chinese Steamers Conscripted 153

To Transport Large Army to Suppress Communists

▲ Wuxue is Extremely Critical

▲ Shangguan Division Ordered to Enter Jiangxi

▲ Merchant Ships Limited to Two Days Arrival

▲ Almost No Chinese Ships on the Yangtze River

The forces of the communist bandits have spread throughout the Yangtze River. Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, personally went upstream to supervise the various armies in suppressing the bandits. He specially convened a meeting of military generals in Lushan to discuss bandit suppression, deciding to mobilize a large army to first clear the traces of bandits in Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei provinces. It is estimated that 15 divisions of troops will be mobilized. Recently, due to the fall of Guangji and the emergency in Wuxue and Luotian, a special telegram was sent to Shanghai to requisition a large number of Yangtze River ships to transport bandit suppression troops. From today onwards, the Yangtze River ships of Chinese merchants in Shanghai will all be suspended. The reporter's investigation is divided into the following summary:

▲ Bandit Alert Along the Yangtze River. Northern Anhui, such as Susong, Taihu, Qianshan, Yingshan, and other places, have been occupied by the communist bandit Kuang Jixun's troops. Huangmei and Guangji have been captured by Gong Bingyan, Li Can and other groups. Residents have fled to Jiujiang and Wuxue. According to refugees who fled to Shanghai by Yangtze River steamer yesterday, Guangji was occupied by the Red Army on the 11th. Due to the mutiny of the garrison troops in Luotian and Qishui, the people are even more panic-stricken, with several alarms every night. The inland areas within 80 miles along the Yangtze River in Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei have almost become bandit areas. Qichun is even more critical. Inland traffic upstream has almost been blocked by the Red Army. In recent days, refugees fleeing to Shanghai have been extremely crowded.

▲ Large-Scale Mobilization. The bandit suppression troops for this Lushan Conference have been designated to be divided into four routes in Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Henan. In northern Anhui, Wang Jun's Seventh Division, Xu Yaoting's Fifth Division, and Yue Shengxian's 46th Division will advance from Anqing, Hefei, and other places, while Hu Zongnan's division will provide support. In Luotian and other places in Hubei Province, Zhang Yinxiang's 31st Division and Ge Yunlong's 33rd Division will be transferred. Ma Hongkui's 35th Division and Guo Rutong's 26th Division will be ordered to garrison Xinyang and cooperate in the attack. Other divisions such as Dai Minquan, Huang Lie, and Cao Wanzhong are also being mobilized.

▲ Troops Transferred to Wuxue. Wuxue is an important place upstream and a must-pass for Yangtze River steamers. Due to the fall of Guangji this time, Wuxue is extremely tense. Chairman Chiang urgently ordered Shangguan Yunxiang's 47th Division, which went south during the anti-Japanese war, to expedite its departure to Jiangxi to rescue Wuxue. After withdrawing from Kunshan, Shangguan's troops were stationed in Changshu. Yesterday, they were ordered to depart for Nanjing and Zhenjiang, and to go west by steamer overnight directly to Jiujiang and Wuxue to suppress the Red Army in Guangji.

▲ Yangtze River Ships Requisitioned. Yesterday, Chiang ordered the Ministry of Military Affairs to requisition all Yangtze River steamers from the Shanghai China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Sanpei, and Ning Shao companies, ordering them to go to Nanjing and Zhenjiang to await dispatch for troop transport. After receiving the order, the three companies temporarily cancelled the scheduled commercial sailings of the various Yangtze River steamers and ordered them to rush to load coal overnight. This morning, more than ten ships, including Jianghua, Ningjing, and Changxing, rushed to Zhenjiang and Nanjing to transport troops west.

▲ Chinese Merchant Ships All Suspended. The Chinese Yangtze River steamers of the three companies were suspended for a long time during the Shanghai war. They had only recently resumed operations when they suddenly received the order to be requisitioned. Yesterday, the ships that had been scheduled to go to Nanjing included Jiangda, Jiangyu, Jiangtian, Jianguo, Jiangxin, Jianghua, Changan, Dexing, Fengpu, Fulong, Ningjing, and others. Four small Yangtze River steamers from the Tongyang route were also dispatched. At that time, it was planned to transfer all Chinese ships on the Yangtze River. After repeated consultations among the three companies, Jiang'an, Jiangshun, and Ning Shao were kept to maintain commercial services and facilitate transportation. As for the ocean-going ships that should be requisitioned, there are also Tonghua, Gongping, Yushun, Taishun, Wanxiang, Hua'an, and Xin Ningxing. The Chinese ships on the Yangtze River and sea routes that remain in operation in Shanghai account for only one-tenth of the total.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company 154

Salary Increase for Engine Department

▲ Company is Considering Improving Treatment

▲ Qualifications and Status Must Also Be Defined

The wages of the staff of the engine departments of various merchant ships of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company were very high during the era of employing foreign engineers. Since the change to Chinese employees, wages have suddenly been reduced. The Engine Association submitted conditions and requested the general manager to improve treatment and increase wages. The latest news investigated is as follows:

▲ Company's Statement. A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency visited General Manager Li Weihou yesterday. According to him, the personnel of the engine department were originally all foreign. In order to recover rights and interests, Chinese personnel were gradually used, mostly coppersmiths and other promoted staff, and their wages were roughly the same as those of Chinese employees in other companies. The case of improving treatment has now been investigated and is being considered. Within the possible scope, and to the extent that the company's financial resources can afford, detailed measures will be reviewed and appropriate increases will be made.

▲ Salary Increase Amount. The General Federation of Engineers requested an increase in salary. According to the statement yesterday, the requested salary amount is: (1) Chief Engineer, originally 160 yuan, please add 20 yuan to 180 yuan, and gradually increase to 300 yuan in the future. (2) First Assistant Engineer, original salary 120 yuan, now please add 10 yuan to 130 yuan, and increase to 180 yuan in the future. (3) Second Assistant Engineer, original salary 80 yuan, add 10 yuan to 90 yuan, and increase to 140 yuan in the future. (4) Third Assistant Engineer, original salary 60 yuan, please add 10 yuan to 70 yuan, and increase to 100 yuan in the future.

▲ Define Qualifications. According to Wang Tong, Chief of the Shipping Department of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the company has no regulations regarding the qualifications and status of engineers. The company is currently discussing the engineers' request for a salary increase, but the general manager has not yet made a statement. However, the shipping department is planning to stipulate the qualifications and status of engineers. Roughly, the position of chief engineer is equal to that of the shipowner's representative, above the first mate. With qualifications defined, there will be a procedure for wages, and the responsibilities of those who hold this position can also be clearly defined.

▲ Recruitment. The six engineering trainees recruited by the company this time have been announced. They are Lu Jingyun, Di Zhaolin, Xu Wei, Lu Zhongxun, Wu Bangyan, and Li Wenchang. A notice was issued yesterday ordering them to report to the company immediately and await assignment to various ships for internships. There is also Zhu Yafang, whose French test paper still needs to be re-examined with an oral examination. These members will be reported by the company to the Maritime Administration Bureau for record. According to Zhou Houkun, the examiner, a second batch of trainees is planned to be recruited.

Murderer Commits Suicide 155

▲ Hengsheng Commits Suicide in Fear of Punishment Yesterday Morning

▲ Heim Can Rest in Peace Underground

The case of the murder of a fellow Westerner in the western Shanghai Lincoln Road, near Warren Road, on the morning of the 17th (the day before yesterday), has been detailed in yesterday's newspaper. However, after the incident, the police quickly and completely investigated the surnames, origins, and professions of the deceased and the murderer. The body of the deceased was examined by the US Assessor's Office yesterday morning, and the US Consulate and the police strictly searched for the murderer. Unexpectedly, the murderer, knowing that he could not escape the law, committed suicide with a gunshot in a Russian apartment at 471 Lafayette Road in the French Concession yesterday morning. The details are as follows:

▲ Deceased Was Only Son. The only eyewitness to the tragedy was Zhao Zhiliang, a Yongbo driver from the United Automobile Company. Therefore, after Zhao reported to the police, the police chief sent personnel to find the body with Zhao Zhiliang. After investigation, it was learned that the deceased was named Heim R.K. Heim, and the murderer was named Hengsheng T.M. Hansen. Both were American citizens. The deceased was only 23 years old and was an only son. His parents are alive and currently live in the United States. He came to China 18 months ago and initially worked for the Meifu Petroleum Company in Tianjin. He came to Shanghai last winter and later joined Puyi Bank. He had just resigned at the beginning of this week and was living in the YMCA on Jing'an Temple Road.

▲ Murderer Passing Through Shanghai on Way Back to America. The murderer, Hengsheng, came to China in 1927 and served as a third-class pharmacist in the US Navy. The following year, he transferred to the Meifeng Bank and was soon transferred to the Tianjin branch to work. This time, he was on his way back to the United States via Shanghai. He arrived in Shanghai a few days ago and stayed at the Duchen Hotel on Sima Road. He was originally scheduled to return to the United States on the President Garfield steamer yesterday morning. It is unknown how the tragedy of assassinating Heim occurred.

▲ US Assessor Examined. Yesterday morning, Kreissel, a magistrate from the US Assessor's Office, along with six jurors, swore an oath at the Assessor's Office and then went with the magistrate and prosecutor to the International Funeral Home. First, they inspected the body of Heim. Dr. Langxi, who had examined the body yesterday, pointed out the bullet wounds. One bullet entered from the upper left thigh and exited from the right chest. One bullet entered from the base of the skull behind the head and exited from the head above the right eye. Both were fatal. They then examined the bloody coat worn by the deceased and went to the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station to interrogate the driver about the assassination situation at that time.

▲ Driver's Eyewitness Account. According to the driver's testimony, he picked up two Westerners at 11:40 yesterday morning. He recognized one of them as an old customer. When the car reached the west of the concession, it traveled south along Lincoln Road. Suddenly, he heard an explosion. At this time, he was driving, and the deceased was sitting on his left. Another Westerner was leaning on the gasoline tank, facing Heim and him. His left hand was holding the gasoline tank, and his right hand was hidden in his raincoat. Before the explosion, the Westerner had told him and Heim to look up at something in the direction of the Brahma King Ferry. When the explosion occurred, he looked back and saw that Heim had fallen on the seat. Previously, the two Westerners had been talking, seemingly friendly and without any grudges. He also did not see a pistol. Afterwards, the other Westerner ordered him to stop the car and asked him to help move Heim's body to the back of the car, saying that he was sick and needed to be taken to the hospital. After moving the body, he returned to his seat and drove. But when he occasionally looked back, he saw the Westerner standing in the car, and the body was gone. When he drove near Warren Road Bridge, the Westerner got out of the car and left. He then drove back to report to the car company and relayed the information to the police station.

▲ Murderer Rented Apartment. After assassinating Heim and fleeing, Heng knew that the police and the US Consulate would definitely be searching everywhere. Since he was an American, he knew that he could not escape the law. He then had the idea of committing suicide. Heng went to the Russian apartment at 471 Lafayette Road in the French Concession alone at around 3:00 pm the day before yesterday, rented a room on the east end of the second floor, and agreed on a monthly rent of 40 yuan. After entering the room, he showed a tired state and ordered the waiter to bring him a glass of cold water. He then closed the door and went to bed. No one saw him again after that.

▲ Committed Suicide with a Gun in Fear of Punishment. At around 8:00 am yesterday morning, a faint groan suddenly came from Heng's bedroom. The boarders in the next room knew something was wrong and told the waiter. The waiter knocked on the door but received no response. He then peeked in through the window gap above the door and saw that Heng had fallen on the bed, his left wrist artery had been cut, and blood was flowing all over the bed. The waiter was horrified and reported to the owner, who relayed the information to the French police station. By the time the detectives arrived, Heng had already shot himself in the forehead and committed suicide. A bottle of poison was also found in his room, which was probably also a tool he used to commit suicide.

▲ US Consulate Sent Personnel to Identify the Body. The French police station initially could not determine the cause of his suicide. After investigation, they learned that he was the murderer in the Heim assassination case and committed suicide in fear of punishment. They immediately notified the Public Concession Police Station, which relayed the information to the US Consulate. Personnel were immediately dispatched to confirm the identity. The body is awaiting examination tomorrow.

Pawnshop Owner's Son 156

Chops and Kills Two Shop Employees

▲ Owner's Son Keeps Company with Thugs

▲ Perpetrator Acts Viciously after Failed Extortion

▲ Three Perpetrators Total

▲ Steals Jewelry and Cash before Leaving

Yesterday at approximately 2:00 PM, three people suddenly came to the Qingfu Pawnshop, number 2649 Yangshupu Road, across from the power plant. They shut the main entrance, and ran into the shop, demanding money from the shop employee, a Mr. Li Guan-nan, who was from Luo Dian. One of them was the pawnshop owner's son. Li attempted to escape through the back door, seeking to find the boss. However, he was grabbed, his chest clothing yanked on, and for no reason, a dagger was pulled out and swung down for seven strikes, one on the throat and one on the abdomen. The scene was covered with blood, and he expired soon after. Another employee, a Mr. Jiang Zhen-Fang of Guangdong, aged twenty-three, tried to persuade those attacking. However, under the owner's son's rage, he was stabbed multiple times, and soon dropped dead due to his injuries. The three took two jewelry boxes from the counter, and paper currency amounting to about two hundred twenty yuan, before escaping through the back door. A young apprentice returned later and saw that the front door was shut tight. Going through the back door, the two corpses were found covered in blood. He cried out, and called neighbors to come. Local police number 2078, and the local patrol, were notified. After investigating, the police determined that the attacker was the owner's son. Since his youth he never pursued an honorable path, indulging in recreational pursuits. His father had repeatedly cautioned him without effect. Last year his father placed an advertisement severing their relationship. Living like a derelict, he ran with hoodlums, and when his finances ran low, he would try to use the pawnshop. This happened monthly, and due to his father's heavy opium addiction, he was bedridden, and all tasks were handed to Li Guan-nan. Li, not tolerating these disturbances, had reported the behavior to the owner, and instructed Li to ignore his son's presence. Because of these actions he grew to hate Li. Therefore, the attack was for revenge. The police are chasing those involved.

Filed a Second Petition to the Municipal Government Yesterday

Public Concession 162

Fire Fighting Work in May

The Fire Brigade of the Public Works Department reported that it received 46 calls this month, including 9 false alarms, 2 false reports, and 4 special calls. The property endangered by fire amounted to Tls. 6,405,550 within the concession and Tls. 143,500 outside the special donation area. The actual losses were Tls. 77,755 and Tls. 20,471 respectively. Ten firefighters were injured, and five others were injured. Nine houses were damaged, none of which were completely destroyed. Firefighters spent 9,557 hours on duty in entertainment venues. The most noteworthy fire this month was the Japanese military transport ship Bombay Maru, which caught fire carelessly while docked at the South Manchurian Railway Pier. The accident occurred in hold No. 4, which stored a large amount of gasoline and kerosene. Hold No. 3 contained a large amount of munitions, and there were also munitions on shore, raising concerns about an explosion. The cables were cut, and the ship was allowed to drift downstream, with fireboats following to provide assistance. The fire was eventually confined to hold No. 4, preventing it from spreading. Firefighters worked for five days and nights and a half before completely extinguishing the fire. Afterwards, the Japanese Navy, Army, and ship personnel cooperated, and customs and tugboat company staff also provided assistance. The Emergency Division of the Ambulance Brigade received 132 calls this month, the highest number ever. A total of 135 people were sent to the hospital, including 47 injured in road accidents, 19 in fights, 16 with sudden illnesses, 9 who fainted, 7 attempted suicides, 3 with burns, 3 with knife wounds, 1 with gunshot wounds, and 5 with unknown causes. Among the other 25, there were 8 men and 27 women. The Hospital Division received 286 calls and sent 311 people to and from the hospital.

Dispute Over Soda and Stamp Tax 165

▲ The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sent a Letter Requesting a Refund

▲ The Stamp Tax Bureau Provided a Detailed Explanation

▲ Official Letter from the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to the Tobacco Exchange Guild: On the 13th of this month, a public letter from the Jiangsu Shangbao Stamp Tax Bureau stated: "Regarding your association's letter No. 568, which included a letter from the Tobacco Exchange Guild stating that Shen Wancheng and Chen Defeng, tobacco exchanges, successively reported being inspected by stamp tax bureau inspectors for selling soda without stamps, identified as tax evasion, and detained to the bureau, etc. The soda is manufactured by factories, and the stamp tax should be collected from the factories. The stores are retailers and have no responsibility to bear the stamp duty. Please uphold justice and alleviate the difficulties of merchants, and write to the tax bureau to return the detained goods first, and clearly stipulate that the factory is responsible for the stamp duty, and announce it to the public, etc. The stamp duty for soda is a special stamp tax, which is a tax on goods, similar to the stamp duty for cigarettes. The responsibility for paying taxes should be on the manufacturers, not the shops. The request of the guild to return the goods detained from the two stores and clearly stipulate the responsibility for stamping is a legitimate request. Please investigate and handle it separately according to the regulations that factories should affix stamps at the factory, and return the detained goods, etc." The Bureau investigates that the soda stamp tax was ordered to continue in April of this year. The Bureau immediately checked the previous year's case and notified the soda industry guild through your association that the factories should affix stamps at the factory to pay taxes and strengthen tax revenue. At the same time, the Bureau notified all factories to affix stamps on all soda leaving the factory and to avoid any omissions that would lead to inspection and detention. In April, a bulletin was widely distributed and posted in public places. The Bureau clearly stated in letters and announcements that the soda stamp tax should be borne by the factory. This is not difficult to review. However, due to the relationship of the Shanghai Concession, there are special circumstances. The soda factories in the Concession may not consistently comply with the method of affixing stamps at the factory, or there may be omissions in the procedures. Therefore, it is necessary to pay attention to inspection. Therefore, in addition to investigating whether there is tax evasion when transporting soda at the junction of the Chinese and Concession areas, the soda shops must also be inspected to investigate whether the factory is implementing the stamping. This is the Bureau's responsibility for collecting taxes and must pay attention to inspection. Now, according to the previous reason, the soda detained from the two tobacco exchange stores, Shen Wancheng and Chen Defeng, has been approved by your association to be returned. In order to alleviate the difficulties of merchants, the Bureau can do so. You should transfer the letter to the Tobacco Exchange Guild and inform the two stores to come to the Bureau to claim it. As for the guild's request to clearly stipulate the responsibility for stamping, the Bureau has notified the soda manufacturers in the Chinese and Concession areas of the method of affixing stamps at the factory, and in April of this year, it sent a letter to your association to inform the soda industry guild to notify all manufacturers to comply. The responsibility for soda stamps has been clearly assigned to the factory. Since it has been stated again and again, there is no need to stipulate it again. I have always admired your association's leadership of the merchants, and the public's opinions are in agreement. If you consider the relationship of national taxes and notify the soda industry manufacturers of the Bureau's original letter in April of this year and persuade them again, it will be seen that borrowing your words will surely lead to a clear effect in the method of affixing stamps at the factory in the future. At the same time, write to the Tobacco Exchange Guild to urge all tobacco exchange stores to pay attention to whether there are any missing stamps when purchasing soda in the future. If there are any unstamped, they must affix stamps on each bottle before selling it. When purchasing goods, do not mistakenly purchase unstamped soda, causing disputes. If this is handled, it will be possible to promote each other on both sides, and both national taxes and commercial conditions will surely benefit more, etc. The guild heard that the guild is firmly opposed to the tax bureau's method of requiring shops to affix stamps on each bottle, and plans to telegraph the head office to request instructions, and plans to send personnel to warn the industry to stop selling, fearing that it will cause a huge turmoil, following the Tianjin's armed resistance.

▲ Discussion: Since Liu Qingzeng, the director of the Shangbao Stamp Tax Bureau, took office, he has been making great efforts to rectify tax collection and seek truth from facts. Regarding the soda stamp tax, he believes that the tax revenue should also improve during the current peak season for soda sales. In order to prevent tax evasion, he invited representatives from various soda factories and companies to consult in detail and discuss it. In view of the established cases, there have been regulations for the soda industry to pay taxes and affix stamps for a long time. He hopes that each company will fulfill its responsibilities in accordance with the regulations to help the process. The representatives were clear about the facts and were willing to comply with the regulations and pay taxes to operate. However, they claimed that when soda is transported to other cities, merchants in each place believe that the soda is sold in a certain place and must use the stamps of that place. There is no need to use the stamps of the place of origin. Director Liu explained to them that the stamp is a national tax. Since there is Shangbao stamp, it is valid for inspection anywhere, and it is not subject to re-taxation. If any omissions are found, the local stamp tax bureau should order it to be supplemented locally. This is the established method. Merchants in other cities may not be fully aware of this misunderstanding. I hope to explain it at any time to dispel doubts. Each representative expressed their willingness to comply after this negotiation.

Robbery on Ximen Road 170

The Stolen Goods Were Taken to the Roof to Escape

▲ Detectives Conducted a Large-Scale Search with No Results

▲ The Entrance of Run'an Lane Was Like Facing a Formidable Enemy

Yang Junmu, a resident of a single-room shikumen house at No. 90 Run'an Lane on Ximen Road in the French Concession, is from Sichuan, 36 years old. He runs the Qing Zihao business on Sima Road, specializing in the transportation and sale of cotton yarn to Sichuan. His mother, wife, and maid are at home. The downstairs is sublet to a three-room tenant, Wu Jingshu and his wife. Yang Junmu returns home from the business at 6:00 or 7:00 PM every day. On the evening before last (the 17th), he had an appointment with relatives, and only his old mother and maid were at home. Unexpectedly, at 8:15 PM, five bandits suddenly broke in through the back door. Three bandits wore gray gowns and bowler hats, and two bandits wore short coats, holding three pistols and speaking with a Sichuan accent. After the bandits entered the door, they first intimidated them into silence, and then drove Yang's mother and the three-room tenants, Wu Jingshu and his wife, into the back parlor, guarded by two bandits. Three bandits went upstairs to ransack boxes and cabinets, wantonly searching and looting. More than 50 yuan in foreign currency, a gold needle worth 32 yuan, and a silver pocket watch and a wristwatch were robbed. There was also an IOU for 400 yuan, which was established by Cheng Zijian on December 17th of the Republic of China. Until around 9:00 PM, the bandits heard the police patrol and escaped with the stolen goods to the roof. It turned out that while the bandits were searching, the Songshan Road Police Station received a phone call from a neighbor in the lane and immediately sent West Inspector Xing Lihua and Inspector Jin Jiulin, leading more than 100 Chinese and foreign detectives, in three trucks and two cars, to Run'an Lane to arrest them. For a while, it was like facing a formidable enemy, and the road was blocked. After the detectives searched the nearby area without success, all the detectives dispersed at 10:30 PM. It is said that the victim has opened a loss report and reported it to the police station.

After Two Bandits Were Arrested 171

Suddenly Pointed Out That the Victim Had Committed Murder

▲ Said to be the Murderer in the Wang Abao Tragedy

▲ Friends Who Went to the Police Station to Inquire Were Also Arrested

At around 6:00 PM on the afternoon of the 16th of this month, six bandits armed with weapons suddenly came to the home of Kong Guangfu, a native of Anhui, at No. 746 Yongji Lane on Weihaiwei Road, intimidating them into silence. They ransacked boxes and cabinets, robbing Kong and his sister-in-law, Kong Wu, of clothing, jewelry, and silver worth 580 yuan, and fled. Afterwards, Kong reported to the Xinzha Police Station based on information, stating that he had known two of the six bandits for a long time, named Zhou Zhongyi and Zhou Zhonghua, two brothers. The police chief then sent Chinese detective Yue Huayou Shan and Western detective Mu Keying to investigate. On the previous day, they finally found out that the two Zhous were hiding at No. 3923 Daxu Lane on Roberts Road and went to arrest the two Zhous and brought them to the police station. Under questioning, they denied being bandits, but confessed that the plaintiff Kong Guangfu was actually a wanted criminal in a murder case, and had shot and killed Wang Abao, the foreman of the Rigao Gunny Bag Factory, in April of the 18th year of the Republic of China. Kong was then arrested. Not long after, Kong's friend Zhang Guomin went to the police station to inquire and was also identified by the two Zhous as a common criminal in the murder case and was also arrested. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. According to the police lawyer Wang Yaotang's statement of the previous situation, the two Zhous were being prosecuted for robbery, but the police had not yet prosecuted the two criminals, Kong and Zhang, for murder and requested permission to detain them in order to investigate evidence. Then, the witness, the woman Kong Wu, filed a complaint about the situation of being robbed by six bandits who broke into the upstairs the day before, and pointed out in court that the two Zhous were present at the time. When questioned, Zhou Zhongyi denied the robbery and suddenly suffered false accusations. He stated that he had known Kong for a long time. This time, a disaster occurred in Shanghai. Kong secretly colluded with the Japanese and acted as a traitor. After I reported it, Kong was sent to the Garrison Headquarters for detention. He was released only now and held a grudge in his heart, falsely accusing me of being a bandit. However, Kong murdered Wang Bao with a pistol several years ago. This matter was told to us by Kong's friend, a certain Wang. Zhou Zhonghua also did not admit to being a bandit. Three years ago, I met Kong on the road, and Kong invited me to his house and entrusted me with murdering Wang Abao because Wang refused to strike. If the matter was successful, he would give a reward of 40 yuan. I refused. Several days later, Wang Abao was shot and killed, which was obviously done by Kong. Questioning Kong Guangfu, he confessed that Zhou Zhongyi did come to his house the day before to rob, and there were six people upstairs. Because the two Zhous organized the workers' union in the 16th year of the Republic of China, and Yu Shi was the cadre of the workers' department of the Municipal Party Department, he knew each other. He did not know about the murder of Wang Abao. After Wang was killed, the Zhou brothers were arrested by the police station, but he did not know how they were released. Zhang Guomin confessed that he used to work with Kong. Yesterday, he heard that Kong was arrested, so he went to the police station to inquire and was also detained. He knew nothing about the murder case. After verification, Judge Wu Tingqi ordered the two Zhous to wait for another hearing on the 25th, and Kong and Zhang were allowed to be detained for seven days.
