Shen Bao Local Supplement

Discussion

Bigamy 186

— Fo

Yesterday, I saw a news story about a wealthy businessman who cheated on a female painter in marriage. The original wife filed for divorce, and the new bride made a big fuss and returned to Ningbo alone. This incident was truly a case of ["a hunchback falling, failing at both ends"], and instead evolved into a family tragedy.

Originally, such tragedies happen every day in Shanghai. It is truly commonplace. This is just one example. The crime of bigamy is clearly stipulated in the law, but people living in Shanghai are often tempted by the environment, or they dislike the old and like the new, or they think of carnal desires when they are well-fed and warm. Therefore, we often see such tragic cases of burning the zither and cooking the crane. Although the law is such, it is not an absolute guarantee. As long as you can get through two conditions:

First, have a special status so that the law can lose its effect.

Second, have absolute financial power, and there will certainly be a way to resolve it.

If you don't have the above two latent forces, not only will your family be in disarray, but you will also be subject to criminal penalties.

Science

Refreshing Straw Hats 189

— Di Lei

Straw hats are a necessary item for summer. Usually, all classes in society each have one. However, our experience with wearing straw hats is that almost every season, when we no longer need them, even if we store them very well, we inevitably have to replace them with new ones next summer. This is because the originally white wheat straw turns into an unsightly yellow or becomes dull and lackluster after a few months. There are many advertisements in the market for refreshing straw hats. Economical friends seem to think it is a pity to discard them, so they spend a few jiao to have them washed. In fact, the discoloration of straw hats can be considered a kind of reduction reaction. The original wheat straw was yellow. After the manufacturing factory made the straw hats, they forcibly bleached them. Naturally, after a certain period of time, they will restore their original appearance. Although I have never opened a straw hat washing shop, based on my experience, I dare to offer an effective and easy method. If the reader is interested, you may want to try it according to the method.

Prepare a basin of clean water, four glass cups, three brushes, oxalic acid, potassium permanganate, and sodium thiosulfate (i.e., large soda) in small amounts. Soak each in a concentrated solution and put them in the cups.

First, wash the straw hat in clean water to remove accumulated dust and dirt in the seams. While the straw hat is not completely dry, use a brush to dip in the potassium permanganate solution and apply it evenly once. The straw hat will be dyed a layer of dark purple color. After applying it well, place it in the sun for about three minutes. Then use another brush to dip in the oxalic acid solution and apply it to the purple hat. As you apply it, brush it. The purple potassium permanganate will react with the oxalic acid, releasing oxygen and bleaching the straw hat. Wash it with clean water, then brush it with the sodium thiosulfate solution, and it will be as white as new. After it is dry, it can be worn.

The principle is that oxalic acid reacts with potassium permanganate to release oxygen, which oxidizes the yellow wheat straw and makes it colorless. After washing, adding sodium thiosulfate can remove the residual acidity (the oxalic acid solution is acidic and cannot adhere to the hat). This very simple method can be completed in a quarter of an hour, and the chemicals only cost a small amount. It is far more economical than replacing it with a new one, and it also seems more economical and very reliable than asking a hat washing shop to wash it.

Note: After brushing the straw hat, it is easy to become uneven when drying. Just press it with a weight before it is dry, and it will be flat. It is best to use several volumes of Western-style books.

Life

Modern Gentleman 190

— Qing Xia

Yesterday, I went to my close friend Mr. Wang's house and saw that his neighbor lived a modern couple. The man was wearing a suit, looking very energetic, and loved to say "Excuse me," "Hello," "Yes," with a sense of abundance in his ears.

According to Mr. Wang, this brother is full of foreign air. There are two things that are quite interesting to talk about.

This brother has a younger sister who is over ten years old. One day, he accompanied her on a public bus to go somewhere. The ticket seller came to sell him tickets, and he only bought one ticket. The ticket seller asked why his sister didn't buy one. He repeatedly said, "Small." What he meant was that girls could ride for free. Coincidentally, the ticket seller didn't understand English, so he said sternly, "We don't care about Fourth Ma Road or Fifth Ma Road, you still have to buy a ticket." Everyone nearby laughed. In the end, he had to buy the ticket.

Another time, his wife went out and hadn't returned, and he felt very lonely. He decided to go see a movie to relieve his boredom. When he was about to leave, he told his nanny, "If Madam comes back and asks about me, you can say 'Cinema'." Who knew that his nanny didn't understand what he meant and thought that he and his wife had turned against each other. Afterwards, she sighed to others behind her back, "Alas! The gentlemen of today are really rude. I never thought that our master in Western clothes would say 'Cao Ni Ma'." It turned out that she had misunderstood "Cinema."

Business Faces

Several Special Faces 191

— Kong Yiping

Postal service employees seem to be all taught by the same master. If you take express mail or registered mail to the post office before 9:00, the masters will talk and laugh freely, letting you wait outside the copper frame for their judgment. After 9:00, they will slowly prepare their work tools and issue receipts for a stack of letters and documents. Sometimes there are too many letters, and if it passes 12:00, no matter how important your letter is, please come again in the afternoon. I'm afraid the slow mail has already been sent to the station.

A rural old woman carrying a package mistakenly stepped into a first-class tram. The ticket seller shouted fiercely, "Go to the back, go to the back!" Because the rural woman was already at the junction of the first three classes, she politely asked the ticket seller, "Sir, thank you, open it a little," hoping that the ticket seller would open the middle door. The ticket seller reluctantly opened the door and let her pass, and slammed the door shut, cursing, "Swine."

"Sir, I'm sorry." Obviously, the payment did not match the invoice, and he already had a smiling face towards people.

The clerks in silk shops and foreign goods stores also have genuine rubber faces. If you are a rural bumpkin, don't pester them this way and that. The old bosses hire them to deal with female customers.

A friend calls and says that his factory needs to add bookkeepers. You go to the writing room before 9:00 tomorrow to meet the boss for an interview. The next day, I rushed to his office, but the boss had not yet arrived. After 9:30, I was sent in to see the so-called boss with a high belly. My friend went to tell him to wait outside because he was busy with official business.

At 11:30, I was summoned into the boss's room. The "interview" only asked the following simple questions.

"Which school did you graduate from?"

"Have you worked after graduating?"

"Do you have experience in bookkeeping?"

"Report to the factory tomorrow!" And signed a pass for me to enter the factory (the writing room is on ×× Road, and the factory is located in Pudong).

In two hours, there was not even a three-minute gap to ask the above questions. Seeing the Louis Stone performing face he had when he asked the questions, it must be the boss's air!

Page 22

Writing

Another Registration Fee 192

— Lu

The girl had just returned from school, and before even putting down her schoolbag, she earnestly said to her mother:

"Mom? The school is asking for another registration fee."

"What?" the mother said, "Another registration fee?" Then she said to me:

"Mr. L! Don't you find it strange? Their school asks for a registration fee every semester."

So I took a slip of paper from the girl's hand, and saw the following printed in lead type:

"As this semester is nearing its end, if student ××× wishes to continue studying at this school in the next semester, it is hoped that

the parents will promptly pay the registration fee of five yuan according to regulations, in order to register. This is to notify you. Sincerely, Principal ××× Attached note: This notification is not to be used as a receipt for money. When the registration fee is paid, the school's accounting office will issue a separate receipt as proof."

At that time, I was simply stunned. I really don't understand, what exactly does this school do? Then the girl said:

"When school was dismissed, the teacher gave everyone a slip like this. She said to bring it at the latest in five days. Everyone has to bring it."

"What strict school rules," I thought. "It must be paid within five days." So the girl's mother angrily said to me in Mandarin:

"This principal is really clever. For example, if you pay this five yuan, then this student is his, and he is sure that you will still pay the tuition. Even if you don't go there again, then at least he gets these five dollars." Then I continued:

"Humph! Five yuan per person, fifty for ten people, five hundred for a hundred people! Ah! That's a really big income!"

"Isn't it?" the mother said again. "Another registration fee, it's simply to get rich!"

Fu Gui

In the article on taking laws from fruit juice, the name Ethyleve was not used. It was found to be due to an error in the article signed by Qing Jun on the method of early ripening of vegetables and fruits. I will not answer on his behalf. At the same time, I also want to know the details, because Ethyle is something whose boiling point is more than 100 degrees below zero Celsius. It is a gas at room temperature. The manufacturing method is very simple, but drug stores probably can't buy it, and it can't be sprayed like a liquid. After the contributor replies, I hope it can be published to explain the question. Yonghuai respectfully replies.

Letter

On the seventh of this month, I read Mr. Shen Zhibin's article "Classification of Rubber Product Manufacturing Methods and Overview of Factories in Our Country" in your publication. The instructions on the four types of vulcanization methods are very detailed, and I am very grateful. However, could you please ask Mr. Shen Zhibin to reveal one or two ingredients for vulcanization? How much of each ingredient is mixed in direct steam vulcanization, such as the sublimed sulfur used for dissolving rubber, and the amount of Shengshilin ingredient? If you want to make the rubber color white, should you add zinc oxide, and how much of each ingredient? Please let me know everything. The success of small industries depends entirely on you, sir. I respectfully wish you good health. Respectfully, Yu Wang Liheng.

Market

▲ Yun He Shan Ren Donates Calligraphy Fans Yun He Shan Ren has been writing for twenty years, and his name has spread throughout the north and south of the Yangtze River. Now, at the request of a friend, Shan Ren is donating one hundred calligraphy fan surfaces, without taking remuneration. Each piece in this city only costs five jiao for handling fees, and eight jiao for other cities (including postage; stamps are accepted). The pieces should be delivered to Ms. Deng Yueying, Room No. 3, 3rd Floor, No. 112 Route Wagner, French Concession, Shanghai. Pieces should be picked up in three days.

▲ Nanjing's "Glamorous Attire Convention" Starting yesterday at the Nanjing Grand Theater, the glamorous attire convention of Shanghai beauties, which is unseen and unheard of, is deeply praised by the audience. During the performance, eight graceful and beautiful young ladies, as beautiful as celestial beings, slowly walked onto the stage, like dancing flowers and butterflies. The thin chiffon nightgowns and swimsuits they wore were all brightly colored and newly styled. The film "The History of Choosing a Husband" also used the competition of beautiful women as its background, and told the story of a young girl who was deeply poisoned by vanity, resulting in the blemish of white jade, which is both sad and lamentable. The theater has already used air conditioning, allowing people to enjoy the grand event and excellent films, and to dispel the benefits of boredom.

▲ Good News for Patients Mr. Gu Zhenhu, a famous doctor in Pudong, specializes in internal medicine for men and women. He came to Shanghai last year and set up a clinic at No. 36 Doushi Street in Nanshi. He returned to his hometown due to the Shanghai war, and has now returned to Shanghai. He still has a clinic at the original address, and also provides two hours of consultation every afternoon to benefit patients.

Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court 193

(Civil Judgment) In the case of Yao Nanji vs. Luo Ganchang over rent arrears and eviction lawsuit (Ruling) The original judgment regarding the rejection of the request for provisional execution is changed. The respondent should be evicted and pay the rent arrears and interest. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by the respondent. ▲ In the case of China Industrial Bank vs. Chang De Jiu Jihao et al. over repayment of pawn money lawsuit (Ruling) The original judgment, except for ordering Chang De Jiu Jihao to repay the plaintiff (i.e., the appellant) 33,085 taels, 3 qian, 6 fen of silver, and interest at 9% per annum from the date of the judgment until the date of repayment, and rejecting the remaining claims of the plaintiff (i.e., the appellant), is changed. The respondent Zhou Weiyu shall be responsible for repaying the aforementioned principal and interest. If Chang De Jiu Jihao and Zhou Weiyu are unable to repay, the respondent Chang De Fa Hao shall be responsible for compensating for the damages. The remaining appeals are rejected. The litigation costs of both instances shall be borne by the appellant for one-third, and the remaining shall be borne by the respondents Chang De Jiu Jihao, Zhou Weiyu, and Chang De Fa Hao. ▲ In the case of Shi Bao Foreign Firm vs. Zhou Linxiang over payment for goods lawsuit (Ruling) The original judgment regarding the amount of compensation is changed. The appellant shall compensate the respondent 1,143 taels, 3 qian, 5 fen of silver. The remaining appeals are rejected. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant.

(Criminal Ruling) In the case of Lin Lubing et al. being sued for embezzlement (Ruling) The trial proceedings in this case are suspended.

(Criminal Judgment) In the case of Li Degong et al. appealing against robbery (Ruling) The original judgment regarding the portions of Li Degong, Mao Changhua, Sun Shaoqing, Wu Xiaowen, Huang Zhizhong, Wang Hongjin, Wang Wensheng, and Ji Xiaosanzi is revoked. Li Degong, as a repeat offender of continuous joint robbery, is sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment; as a repeat offender of joint snatching, is sentenced to three years of imprisonment; as a repeat offender of theft, is sentenced to two years of imprisonment; to be executed for a total of fifteen years of imprisonment. Ji Xiaosanzi, as a repeat offender of continuous joint robbery, is sentenced to fourteen years of imprisonment. Mao Changhua, Sun Shaoqing, Wu Xiaowen, Huang Zhizhong, Wang Hongjin, and Wang Wensheng are each sentenced to ten years of imprisonment for continuous joint robbery. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be used to offset one day of imprisonment for every two days. ▲ In the case of Tang Shenyu appealing against embezzlement (Ruling) The appeal is rejected. ▲ In the case of Mao Yusheng et al. appealing against false accusation (Ruling) The appeal is rejected. ▲ In the case of Ge Songlin appealing against robbery (Ruling) The original judgment regarding the crimes and punishments of Ge Songlin is revoked. Ge Songlin, as a repeat offender of continuous robbery, is sentenced to fourteen years of imprisonment; as a repeat offender of continuous snatching, is sentenced to three years of imprisonment; to be executed for a total of sixteen years of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be used to offset one day of imprisonment for every two days. One pistol and one magazine are confiscated.

(Public Notice) In the case of Zhou Xuehai vs. Yuan Moqin in a divorce lawsuit appeal, this court has scheduled a public hearing on August 18 at 9:30 a.m. The defendant appellant Yuan Moqin is hereby ordered to appear in court on time to argue the case without delay. This public notice is hereby served. The respondent Yuan Moqin is hereby notified.

Xue Xinxin (i.e., Xue Xingxing), Qiu Yuqing, Gu Tianbao, Lu Amao, Zhou Taomin, and Wang Shenshi are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. The number of days Zhou Ajiu, Guan Abao, Qiu Yuqing, Lu Amao, and Wang Shenshi were detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days. Xue Xinxin, Gu Tianbao, and Zhou Taoshi are given a three-year suspended sentence. The opium paraphernalia is confiscated according to the list.

▲Police Department v. Ren Zhaosheng et al., opium case (Main text): Ren Zhaosheng is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing premises for others to smoke opium substitutes. Zhu Meiyu and Yu Asheng are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days. The opium pipes, opium lamps, red pills, etc., are confiscated and burned according to the list.

▲Police Department v. Chen Fusheng, theft case (Main text): Chen Fusheng is sentenced to four months of imprisonment for stealing the property of others. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days. A two-year suspended sentence is granted.

▲Police Department v. Fu Akang et al., opium case (Main text): Fu Akang is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing premises for others to smoke opium substitutes. Tao Baozu and Xu Sannv are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days. The opium pipes, etc., are confiscated and burned.

▲Police Department v. Xiao Xingru, opium case (Main text): Xiao Xingru is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for selling opium substitutes, and is also fined one thousand five hundred yuan. If the fine is commuted to imprisonment, it shall be calculated at a rate of two yuan per day, but shall not exceed one year. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days. Four packages of white powder and three bottles of white medicinal powder, twenty-seven pounds of red pills, fifteen and a half folded booklets, four account books, one seal, one hundred and thirty yuan in silver dollars, three half-yuan silver coins, three thousand five hundred double-mao coins, one thousand seven hundred and fifty single-mao coins, thirty-one yuan in paper money, twenty-three half-yuan corner tickets, one thousand one hundred and fifty two-jiao notes, five hundred one-jiao notes, and two thousand eight hundred copper coins are all confiscated.

▲Police Department v. Zhuang Awu, opium case (Main text): Zhuang Awu is fined thirty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If he is unable to pay, he shall be detained for one day for every two yuan. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, one opium needle, and one opium tray are all confiscated and burned.

▲Police Department v. Huang Wangshi, opium case (Main text): Huang Wangshi is fined thirty yuan for possessing opium substitutes and opium paraphernalia. If she is unable to pay, she shall be detained for one day for every two yuan. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, one opium needle, one opium ramrod, and one opium tray, as well as two red pills, are all confiscated and burned.

▲Police Department v. Lin Zhaotai, opium case (Main text): Lin Zhaotai is fined one hundred and twenty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If he is unable to pay, he shall be detained for one day for every two yuan. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. Three opium lamps, three opium trays, five opium pipes, twenty-four opium bubbles, and one opium pot are all confiscated and burned.

▲Police Department v. Wang Agen, theft case (Main text): Wang Agen is sentenced to twenty days of detention for theft. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the detention at a rate of one day for every two days. One small pair of scissors is confiscated.

▲Police Department v. Cai Zhaoxiang, damage case (Main text): This case is not accepted.

▲Police Department v. Cai Zhaoxiang, damage case (Main text): This case is not accepted. Cai Zhaohai is fined sixty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia and opium substitutes. If he is unable to pay, he shall be detained for one day for every two yuan. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium license, one opium ramrod, one opium tray, and one opium box of red pills, as well as one pound of red pills, are all confiscated and burned.

▲Police Department v. Wang Agen, theft case (Main text): Wang Agen is sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for the crime of repeated theft. The sentence to be executed is one year and seven months of imprisonment. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days.

▲Plaintiff Cai Keming v. Zhu Youjun, stolen goods case (Main text): Zhu Youjun is found not guilty.

▲Police Department v. Yang Agen et al., assault case (Main text): Yang Agen and Wang Kunming are each sentenced to thirty days of detention for the crime of joint assault. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the detention at a rate of one day for every two days.

▲Plaintiffs Gao Yuqing et al. v. Luo Haitao, defamation case (Main text): This case is not accepted.

▲Police Department v. Zhang Kangxian, theft case (Main text): Zhang Kangxian is found not guilty.

▲Plaintiff Qian Yuezhu v. Chen Zhixin, abandonment case (Main text): This case is under the wrong jurisdiction and should be transferred to the Jiangsu Shanghai Local Court for trial.

▲Police Department v. Chen Laosi, robbery case (Main text): Chen Laosi is sentenced to one year and nine months of imprisonment for the crime of breaking into a residence at night and attempting to commit robbery with accomplices. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days.

▲Police Department v. Wu Lushi et al., opium case (Main text): Wu Lushi, i.e., Teng Lushi, is sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined forty yuan for providing premises for others to smoke opium for profit. Gao Heshang is sentenced to three months of imprisonment and fined thirty yuan for assisting in providing premises for others to smoke opium for profit. Zhu Meiqing, Chen Ziming, Li Aming, Pei Shuqi, and Ren Hesan are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined ten yuan for each committing the crime of smoking opium. If the fines are commuted to imprisonment, it shall be calculated at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days. Zhu Meiqing and Pei Shuqi are given a two-year suspended sentence. The opium paraphernalia, opium, etc., are confiscated according to the list.

▲Criminal Directive: One case where Huang Maifa sued Qian Ayu for theft and requested a supplementary judgment. Upon reviewing the current Code of Criminal Procedure based on the submitted petition, there is no provision for supplementary judgments. The request is not in accordance with the law and cannot be approved. If the litigant is dissatisfied with the original judgment, they may appeal according to the law. Let it be known.

▲Civil Judgment: Fang Erzhe v. Jia Zhaoxiong, bill of exchange case (Main text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff three hundred and thirty yuan for the bill of exchange. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Li Hongchang et al. v. Yong'an Real Estate Company, rent increase case (Main text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲Xu Guitang v. Xue Xianggen, loan case (Main text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff one hundred and thirty yuan and four jiao. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Peng Jincheng v. Liu Jinsheng, compensation for damages case (Main text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲Ruihua Company Zhang Hanzhong v. He Juqing, rent arrears case (Main text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff five hundred and thirteen yuan in rent. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant for two-thirds and by the plaintiff for one-third.

▲Xielong Real Estate Agency v. Xu Youliang et al., rent arrears and eviction case (Main text): The defendant Xu Youliang shall pay the plaintiff five hundred and sixty taels of silver in rent and ten yuan for cleaning. The defendant Huang Shu'an shall pay the plaintiff two hundred and eighty taels of silver in rent and five yuan for cleaning. The defendant Fu Zizhang shall pay the plaintiff two hundred and fifty taels of silver in rent and five yuan for cleaning. The lease agreement between the defendants and the plaintiff shall be terminated immediately, and the defendants shall vacate the premises. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants in proportion.

▲Zhou Xiegang v. Zhou Rusong, partnership shares case (Main text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲Lin Jianzhao v. You Zanhout, deposit case (Main text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲Bai Qinsheng v. Gu Xinji, guarantee debt case (Main text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff one hundred and fifty yuan on behalf of the Wang surname. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Hua Yonggen v. Tang Fushou, goods case (Main text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff three hundred and thirty-nine yuan for the goods, as well as simple interest at an annual rate of five percent from the date of filing the lawsuit until the date of final execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. The plaintiff's request for provisional execution is dismissed. (June 18)
